                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
Crossing the Hill  
There are many hills we must cross in our lifetime. There are hills in our daily lives, and in our youth, there are also hills. When we have a family and lead it, there are hills to cross, and in social life, there are hills as well. In other words, from the individual to society and to the nation, there are hills that can determine our fate. The same applies when we look at the world.  
The criteria for the success and failure of human history  
From this perspective, you must understand that all matters are connected around a single peak, which is the hill. We often say that someone has succeeded and someone else has failed. So, who is the person said to have succeeded? It is the person who has crossed the hill they aimed for. And who is the person said to have failed? It is the person who could not cross that hill. In our lives, if we achieve what we aim for, we are successful; if we do not achieve it, we are failures.  
When we apply this to history, if history fails to reach the goal it desires through its course, it results in failure, and when it surpasses that standard, it succeeds. This was spoken on April 8, 1970, at 8 PM, at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
* This message was given at the 10th graduation ceremony of the Seonghwa Students.  
8   Crossing the Hill  
In this perspective, when God's providence is viewed, when God fulfills His purpose, He can enter the realm of victory; when He does not, He falls into the realm of failure. From this viewpoint, the providence of restoration, or returning, is necessary in the realm of failure, not in the realm of victory.  
What is a fallen human? They are the descendants of the defeated. So how do these descendants overcome the sorrow of the defeated? This issue becomes a lifelong task that we must struggle with from the moment we are born until our life ends. Therefore, when viewed more broadly, this becomes a societal task, a national task, a global task, and also a task that humanity must resolve for eternity. Whether we can solve this task or not will determine whether human history succeeds or fails. In other words, we must understand that the issue of whether God fulfills the purpose of providence or not is at stake.  
How will we cross the hill of 6,000 years of restoration today?  
When we consider our individual selves today, we cannot help but think about what position we are in. In this moment of receiving our certificates at the 10th graduation ceremony, we must reflect on what position we are in concerning the goal that the providence aims for. We are running towards the peak that the providence aims for, but the paths are diverse. Some go this way, some go that way, and my closest friend may want to go that way while I want to go this way. Given this diverse environment, we must critically examine what path we are taking towards the peak.  
In taking such a path, it is extremely dangerous for someone who does not clarify their direction while also not confirming their position. Such a person will not even see the approaching peak of the hill and will suffer the sorrow of the defeated. They will also fall without knowing the goal they are heading towards.  
So how will we cross that peak? This is the question. By overcoming this hill, the purpose of believing in and following the Unification Church will be fulfilled. We stand today on the foundation of our efforts over the past several years. From this perspective, you must reflect on what position you are in now and reaffirm your stance from your own perspective, not from that of a third party. You must realize that you are facing such a significant issue.  
The hills that our ancestors could not cross are approaching us  
When observing the path of the providence of restoration, there are hills that individuals must cross. The history of the past 6,000 years has been a history to find the lost Adam. It has taken 6,000 years to find a completed man. Only by crossing that hill, where a person has completed and personally triumphed, can we finally meet the time to establish new connections. That time is the era of hope that humanity desires today. Furthermore, the one who must come to this earth as a completed man is the Savior that all people long for, and this idea is the concept of the Savior and the Messiah.  
How many hills must individuals cross in the restoration process throughout history? From the era of servants to the era of servants of servants, from the era of adopted children to the era of sons, Jesus came to this earth but could not fulfill the purpose. Since that day, a painful struggle has continued for 2,000 years. Moreover, without shedding blood, there is no way to pave the path of death, and to cross the hills that individuals must cross, heaven, earth, and humanity have been mobilized. How serious must the fate of humanity be in finding the moment to look towards the peak?  
This hill is the peak that humanity must cross, regardless of whether they like it or not, risking history and eternity. If we cannot cross this hill, the sorrow of a thousand years will lie before us, and the powers of darkness will oppress us in proportion to what we hope for. This is the terrifying historical hill.  
Towards this peak, countless prophets and ancestors have hidden their identities, shed blood, and forgotten their existence in the bloody battles of death, yet they have not achieved their purpose. You must understand that the hill they left unfulfilled is now approaching us. The hill that God has wanted to cross for 6,000 years is now approaching us in this final era of history.  
The Unification Church proclaiming family salvation  
Until now, religions have been for the salvation of individuals. This has been a hill that religions have sought to cross throughout history. So what hill is there after crossing the hill of the individual? There is the hill of the family.  
What kind of church is the Unification Church today? The Unification Church is not a church aiming for individual salvation. It must become a religion that seeks to save families, breaking away from the religious forms that have focused on individual salvation for 6,000 years. This is the historical task that the Unification Church must resolve in the future.  
Today, the state honors individuals. They commend loyal subjects and virtuous sons and daughters, but this is merely honoring individuals, not families. No state has ever honored families at its center. Similarly, there has been no religion that has come out with the goal of family salvation. Without true families, there can be no true nations, and without true nations, there can be no true world.  
Many religions that have emerged through historical processes have not been able to rise to the position of establishing nations. Why? Because their purpose of salvation has been individual salvation. They have not aimed for social salvation or national salvation. They have only aimed for individual salvation as the purpose of religion.  
Religions until now have worked to cross the victorious hill centered on individuals for 6,000 years. However, the path that our Unification Church must take has the hill of the family ahead. To cross this hill of the family, one cannot do it alone. It must be crossed together. In crossing together, it must be done in a lateral relationship, not a front-and-back relationship. This is because the fall occurred due to following. In other words, Eve followed the archangel, and Adam followed Eve, leading to their downfall. In such a following position, salvation cannot be established. Only by going side by side, in an equal position, can relative salvation be established.  
From this perspective, what must the Lord, who comes as a man, do when He comes to this earth? Is it to find a partner who can follow Him and unfold the ideal of the Kingdom of Heaven? That is not enough. He must stand before God together with a partner in a parallel position. Without a man and a woman who can do this, one cannot return to their original state. In other words, without such humans, namely men and women, one cannot cross the hill of the peak they must go over. That is why Jesus said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the brides."  
What kind of formation must we have to cross the hill of indemnity?  
The bride and groom do not go in a front-and-back relationship but in a lateral relationship. When the wedding ceremony is held, there must be an officiant. The bride and groom move forward in parallel in front of them. This is the path of the bride and groom.  
Has there ever been a time in the historical path where one man and one woman walked in parallel before God? No, there has not. This has finally reappeared in the historical path, and it is the final hill that men and women must cross today. Once this hill is crossed, a peaceful family that has never existed in history, a new family that has never existed in history, will be established.  
When such a family is formed, the next step is for the family to go the way centered on the couple. In that family, there will be sons and daughters centered on the couple. These sons and daughters must also not be in a position of following their parents. They must go before God by separating into the father's side and the mother's side while maintaining parallelism. This is the purpose of creation that God desires.  
Thus, there are hills that individuals must cross, hills that couples must cross, and hills that families must cross. If all families cross that hill and become completed families, many families around the world will establish horizontal relationships centered on God, forming a horizontal formation. In this way, families that can each claim their own before God will emerge. When that happens, God will welcome those families with the same blessing and the same joy. However, when in a front-and-back relationship, there will inevitably be sorrow corresponding to the differences.  
Therefore, to establish ideal families in the future, you must understand that men and women who can align horizontally centered on God are necessary. Then, how will such couples lead their children in a lateral horizontal line? This is the question. They must form one family, one lineage, one nation, and one state. If all humanity can walk in this position, then that nation will be the nation that God envisioned! The highest purpose standard that God created on this earth is for all people to appear in the same form in a straight line.  
From this perspective, when we look at our hearts and bodies, it is the same. A person whose heart leads their body cannot stand before God. Such a person cannot fulfill the history of indemnity. So how will you create yourself to be able to lead your heart and body in a lateral line, from the left and right positions? You must fight to create such a self. This fight is an important battle in pioneering your individual path, is it not? Therefore, the question is how you will cross that hill.  
If today God has a purpose in sending the teacher to this earth, is it to welcome the group that follows in a straight line behind the teacher? No. Such a group will be attacked by packs of wolves at some point. They have already moved beyond the observable field of vision. The place where I can directly govern is not behind. I cannot govern behind. To govern behind, I must turn back. To turn back, I must change direction.  
Thus, I must stand within the 180-degree zone to have a protective sphere. Management begins from the 180 degrees. Even when we look at our hands, we are meant to govern within the 180-degree zone. Our eyes do not look behind. When the eyes look straight ahead, the angle gradually narrows. The bridge of our nose is the same. All of this indicates a line that can normally proceed straight.  
From this perspective, believers of the Unification Church, especially you who are graduating today, how are you going? Are you following behind, or are you walking in a parallel line?  
We must cross the hill of eight stages.  
A person of character fulfills and practices what they have promised. If someone says, "I will not follow this because you claimed it was a promise," then that person is not a person of character. The law is based on public standards and promises. Therefore, all people within the promise of the law must observe that law. When the person who made the promise cannot keep the law, they must be sanctioned by the communal law. This is the responsibility of those who must abide by the law.  
Regardless of who made the claim, the established promise must be practiced. If it is not practiced, one becomes a dropout. A promise must be consistent with the promised standard, whether it is a line or a dot. There must be no front-and-back relationship involved. Therefore, when it is said, "We will meet at a certain time," that specific time must be unified. At that point, anyone must stand in the same position. From there, new history begins. It is not achieved in a front-and-back relationship.  
Similarly, when we look at the Unification Church today, there are many hills that the Unification Church must cross. There are hills that must be crossed as individuals, as families, and...
There are hills to be crossed as individuals, there are hills to be crossed as tribes, there are hills to be crossed as nations, and there are hills to be crossed on a global scale. We must cross these hills. The profound meaning of the restoration of the Heavenly Parent requires us to overcome eight stages of hills, starting from the individual level.

So how will we cross these hills? The question is how firmly you are prepared to cross them yourselves. Those who cannot go even if told to go will ultimately not be able to go. Similarly, those who cannot come even if told to come will also not be able to come.

Then, whose church is the Unification Church that you believe in? This is not the teacher's church. It is your church and my church. Whose ideology is the ideology of the Unification Church? It is not the teacher's ideology. If it were only the teacher's ideology, it would be a sin against all humanity. This is the ideology of all people, as well as the ideology of the citizens of the Republic of Korea. Therefore, a country that pursues such an ideology is not just the country of its ancestors. It can also be the country of one's father and my country. This is fundamentally parallel. It belongs to no one.

From this perspective, you must clearly understand what position you hold as young people in the Unification Church. Are you going as an individual, or are you going on behalf of your family? If you are going on behalf of your family, you must manage that family so that it can go straight. Or if you are going for your lineage, you must manage that lineage so that it can go in the same direction. You must put your family or lineage in front of you and cross over.

You may have heard of Jesus being likened to a shepherd who tends sheep or a good shepherd. In times of peace, the shepherd leads the sheep from the front, but in dangerous times, he drives them forward. Today, we are fighting with the world of Satan behind us, so we must place them in front and lead them. Those who do not stand in such a position can never be on the side of heaven. Thus, we must cross the hills that individuals must cross, and we must cross the hills that families must cross.

So what is the Unification Church striving for today? It aims to cross the personal hills, the family hills, the tribal hills, the national hills, and the global hills. Until now, we have been in a position to unite tribes and cross the national hills. 

Do you have the direction to align yourselves with that? If you fail and cannot go down this path, you will not only suffer the sorrow of personal defeat but also the sorrow of national defeat.

If such a person goes to the spirit world, it will be worse than if they had never known, and they will deeply regret it. Spirits in hell can give up because they did not know at all. However, if God has prepared the final time for us to cross the national hill of restoration and we fail to take responsibility and miss this time, it will be a serious problem. Therefore, the Unification Church is not just about knowing.

If the whole is striving to cross the national hill of restoration and you could cooperate with that but did not participate, then for you, the national hill will be the last. However, if you stand in a position of loyalty and cross the national hill, then the path that the church is taking, the path of its purpose, can follow the world’s path and go toward the heavenly path. However, if you are in a situation where you must cross the national hill and cannot go, you cannot pave the way to the world or heaven. You will not be able to receive benefits.

Seek first the kingdom and its righteousness
The longer you have been in the church, the more recognition you should receive. However, if you have been in the church for a long time but are not aligning with God, your sense of responsibility will gradually diminish. In that case, you will be worse off than those who have just joined.

You do not know when you will die. In the age of national providence, if you do not cross the hill you must cross in this environment where you know the will of providence and the responsibilities presented by God, then that will be your end. No matter how hard you try, you cannot go beyond the national hill to the world.

Many people have lived and died from a flat perspective, but did they live centered on the public good? That public good is not just for the country. A public standard that only serves the country will disappear if the country falls. That is why we are told to follow the way of the sages. So who are the sages? Those who live for the world rather than for the country are the sages. And what is the way of the sages, the teachings of the sages? It teaches how to live centered on a global public standard. Why? Because even if a country falls, the world remains.

From this perspective, today our Unification Church is a church that lives for heaven and earth. It is a church that represents history. If the Unification Church has lived like this until now, the issues are different. Within that world, there are countries, there are nations, there are tribes, there are families, and there are individuals. Therefore, those who live for the world can be recognized by all at once as their value standard.

No matter how many mountains a climber has not climbed or how many hills they have not crossed, if they reach the summit of Mount Everest, the highest mountain in the world, that one achievement resolves everything. Even if they have not climbed many mountains until now, through that one action, they can stand on equal footing with countless climbers who have climbed many mountains.

That is why Jesus said, “You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind.” (Matthew 22:37) And then He said, “Do not be anxious about what you will eat or what you will drink or what you will wear. But seek first the kingdom and its righteousness.” (Matthew 6:31-32) So what is that kingdom? It is a country that has a heart to love God, a country that God wants to love. That kingdom refers to the world. What is that righteousness? It is the principle of living in accordance with the predetermined path.

In this restoration process, as well as in your life journey, there are many hills to cross, and how will you cross these hills? This is the task given to you in the future.

Now is the time to make the final decision
What is the position our church aims for today? It is the position of making the final decision that comes only once. However, if you miss that moment, live centered on your own thoughts, and lose it through your own actions, you must not do that. If you lose that, you will become a foolish person who meaninglessly loses the present moment, which holds infinite value in this historical process. Such a person will not be able to claim a glorious victory on that day. In other words, they will not be raised by God as a victorious hero who has crossed the hill in the providential course of God.

That is why we must have a clear purpose. Even if I die, I will die on this path. I will definitely go this way. No matter what the world says, no matter what anyone says beside me, I must be busy going my way. Whether it is night or day, it is a path I must take without rest. Therefore, it is a busy path. Even if I am tired, I must go. Even if I am exhausted, I must go again. It is not just about going alone; I must influence my environment and lead those who follow me. Those who bear such responsibility will be remembered by God.

So, is crossing such hills something that only individuals do? No. If only individuals cross, that person is lonely. Families must also be crossed over. Those of us who are left with the fate of restoration must cross that hill anyway. No one will cross it for you. No one will save you. You must cross it yourself. You must decide on the 5 percent of authority given to you. I must cross that hill and find what belongs to me.

That is why Jesus died on the cross. This was not because God could not save Him. There was a hill that Jesus had to cross. Jesus had a hill to cross in order to choose a bride. If Jesus had welcomed a bride and formed a family, that family would also have hills to cross. And if that family was established before God, there would be hills to cross to connect the tribe centered around that family. Thus, there is a heavy environment of restoration waiting for us. When you think of this, if there are those among you who think they can cross the hill of restoration while treating it as a game or a spectacle, that person is extremely foolish.

To stand on the side of good
You must have a resolute determination. Why must it be so? What is good and evil? Good is on the side of heaven, and evil is on the side of Satan. Today, those of us who are following God on the path of restoration must only stand on the side of good. It must be so. We must not stand on the side of evil. When looking at this fallen land today, was I born on the side of good? No. Am I living on the side of good? No. Every action, every word, every thought, and every deed is rooted in evil, and I am living my life buried in that.

Then how small is the standard of good here? It is merely a speck. To become a person on the side of heaven, the standard of good must be greater than the standard of evil. So when can God manage? When good is small, God cannot intervene. Therefore, the balance of good and evil must be similar within the buffer zone for God to have the right to manage. This is the teaching of the principle.

The tree of the knowledge of good and evil represents the two worlds. What does that mean? It means that it has become the middle position of good and evil. Then who must decide the direction of good and evil? You must decide for yourself. To do that, you must crush evil, defeat Satan, and hold onto God. You must hold onto God with several times more strength than you use to strike Satan. To strike evil, you must exert all your strength. At the same time, you must hold onto God with even greater strength.

That is why the path of restoration is the path of indemnity, and the path of indemnity is a war of attrition. If Satan demands a hundred, you must strike with a force corresponding to a hundred. After that, you must hold onto God with a force greater than a hundred. This cannot be done with just human strength. It is possible because the absolute God grants 95 percent cooperation.

There must be adventure. You must take risks and break through this path. When you think this is the end and throw your life into striking Satan, God will always be with you in that position. You may not know such things. When you reach the final point of taking risks, God will surely be with you. Outside of that position, God cannot be with you. This is the perspective of the principle.

Today, the Korean Peninsula is divided north and south around the 38th parallel. Do you know the fact that in this era of doctors, captives were liberated? They were placed in a middle position and told to choose as they wished. Who holds the right to choose? It is neither the North nor the South. It is only what they themselves hold.

So, are you individuals who can hold more weight in that world? Right now, you are neither this nor that. You must place yourself on a horizontal scale and weigh whether the right side, which is good, is stronger or the left side, which is evil, is stronger. If the left is heavy, you are on the side of Satan. Also, do my eyes look at the world or look at heaven? If I am looking at the world, that is also on the side of Satan. Those eyes must rot. That body must also rot. It must become food for Satan. The person who looks at heaven must win.

Then today, when we say let’s cross the hill, where does the starting point for crossing the hill lie? It is determined by whether the weight of good is large or small. Those who have not yet discerned this are all on the side of Satan. That is not even a problem. So where do you stand? You must think about this. Where do you stand?

Because you were born into a world centered on materialism, the normal path that religion must take is to start from complete denial. So what must you completely deny? You must deny everything from your parents to your siblings, society, country, and the world. If you do not do that, you cannot separate from Satan. 

Therefore, when you completely deny yourself, a second self that can stand on the side of good will arise. You must enter such a realm.

Starting and conquering the summit
When you feel a value greater than being able to sever ties with loving parents, you will become that much closer to God. You must stand in a position where you can correct all your desires for yourself, your country, and this world into desires for God. Only then can you start on the side of heaven. Otherwise, you cannot go toward the summit of restoration that you must cross. You cannot even start. Even if you have started, you will not be able to progress and will end up going in circles.

That is why you must firmly establish this concept in your living sphere. Why do I go to school? Why do I study? The purpose must be clear. The people of the world go to university to solve their own living problems and to succeed in the world. However, our purpose is different. We must know more and become heavenly warriors to restore this country and this nation. Those who study to prepare themselves both inside and outside as heavenly warriors will be taken care of by God. If not, if you eat everything you want, play everything you want, and do everything you want while indulging in pleasure, neither will work. God does not cooperate with those who play in both worlds. Therefore, you must choose between the two.

What kind of person is wise? A wise person is one who makes good judgments. Unification Church members must become wise people. If you know the principle, each of you will clearly know the path you must take. You will clearly understand what time it is. It is not a vague understanding; it is a formal and clear understanding. The position you are in is not a trivial one. After understanding this clearly, you must make a new start. Once you have started, you must go straight toward the goal that God is guiding. You must not think of another path. Otherwise, there are many hills that you cannot cross.
You need to understand this. 
If you think that if you fail while going along the path of your purpose, you can just prepare again and try again, that thought is wrong. If an athlete has fallen behind in the final battleground, the more prestigious the competition, the less likely anyone will recommend that athlete for future competitions. Therefore, once you start, you must take it seriously. You must be willing to risk your life. 
Similarly, as you live your life or walk the path of faith, the question is how you will overcome the challenges that lie ahead. Therefore, you must overcome those challenges. Do not follow others in overcoming them. Those who only move when commanded by a teacher or only get up when scolded are no different from those in the other world. They are merely living by watching. 
We have the paths of individual restoration, family restoration, tribal restoration, national restoration, and world restoration ahead of us. If there is a path to be loyal to the world rather than to our own country, we must be loyal to the world. In that sense, missionaries are close to receiving global blessings. 
From this perspective, what challenges will you overcome in the future? What challenges are you currently facing? Have you reached a destination, or are you merely looking at the challenges, or are you not even doing that? You must clearly define your position. 
To start overcoming challenges, you must distinguish between good and evil. You must establish a foundation for living from the perspective of good, even if it means dying on the right side, which is aligned with heaven. You must lay the groundwork for a life that can do so and make a resolution. When you set out with a new goal, if you are an individual as God has presented, you can normally overcome personal challenges; if you are a family, you can overcome familial challenges; if you are a nation, you can overcome national challenges. Here, whether you can overcome those challenges or not depends on the resolution you have made. Thus, the question arises: how will you overcome those challenges? 
Fulfill your mission as a person of restoration 
You have, of course, come this far following your purpose, but the path you must take in the future is even more important. The term "restoration student" itself can represent the history of our church. The larger that foundation is, the greater the problem becomes. The way you are going will influence countless people who will follow in the future. If you are in a position where you must overcome challenges but fail to do so and cannot fulfill your responsibilities, you will receive a tenfold or a thousandfold intensified judgment. Therefore, even those who have come from restoration backgrounds do not believe in those who have fallen behind or are problematic figures. 
Those from restoration backgrounds represent the church. Among the candidates for blessings this time, whether one is from a restoration background has become an issue. I have seen many ask each other whether they are from a restoration background, regardless of being male or female. Still, seeing many who want to believe in those from restoration backgrounds, you must recognize how serious your position is. 
You must become individuals who can contribute to the church without being a burden as the church faces the challenges ahead. Only then will there be a path for you to go towards your nation, state, or the world in the future. However, if you become a burden, those who are overcoming the challenges of the nation and the world will not want to carry burdens. Those who are burdensome will be left behind in overcoming challenges. 
From this perspective, you must be the ones who overcome your respective challenges. This is the will of the church and the path of restoration, so from now on, each of you must make a new resolution and clarify what position you are in to restart. Do you understand? "Yes." Let us pray. 
<Prayer> Father, today your providential will is passing by. I must become someone who feels your will in my cells and takes on the responsibility to walk step by step toward the summit you desire, regardless of what anyone else says. We often forget this aspect of ourselves. 
Father, about 40 graduates of the 10th restoration class are present here. Among them, how many can be counted as people in your heart? Is there anyone you expect to be able to trust? If one has come to this place in such a pitiful state that they cannot even trust themselves, that itself is miserable, and we cannot help but feel it is extremely pitiful for our church. Father, please forgive us. 
Surely, humans must go. We understand that the path of restoration cannot be traversed without going through the path of pioneering. Now, as members of the Unification Church, we must do our utmost to overcome the personal challenges, family challenges, tribal challenges, national challenges, and even the challenges of the state. May they stand in a position where they do not become a burden but can contribute. 
Before the church can go, we must be the ones who step forward first, knowing that this is the normal path. We sincerely hope and wish that we may be children who comply with your will. 
Remember your children who have endured until now, and let them reaffirm their hopes for tomorrow in their hearts. Allow them to be your sons and daughters who can vigorously overcome the challenges that lie ahead in their life journey, in line with your will. So that we may meet again at the final victory and become a source of joy for you, and that we may be your sons and daughters whom you can proudly present, we sincerely ask for your blessings. 
May you take care of everything today, and may you also take care of all future lives, so that we may be your children who can overcome the historical challenges you lead. We pray all these things in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
2) The Path of Pioneers 
<Prayer> Countless humans until now have flowed through history without knowing the direction. We realize that the prophets and ancestors who have passed through this land have left behind a path of sorrow. Even among them, they were meant to hold onto the heart of your love and walk along with your circumstances, but when we realize that there were no such humans, we come to understand that your position is one of unavoidable suffering, and that it is a pitiful state beyond anything lost on this earth. 
Those who have not experienced the sorrow of losing a son cannot understand the heart of a parent who has lost a son, and those who have not experienced the sorrow of losing a daughter cannot fathom the sorrow of a parent who has lost a daughter. We must become children who say, "Father! Call me." Such thoughts and the sorrow of losing such children do not vanish in an instant. They do not flow away but remain on this earth with time. We come to feel that you are entangled in such dire circumstances, in the most miserable position. 
Today, there are many who say they follow and believe in you, and many religions that serve you, but there are none who wish to live with you and share in your suffering. Many people have the immature mindset of wanting to serve you while transferring all their suffering to you and freeing themselves from pain. We know that we must not become such people. 
Where are the sons who can hold onto your broken heart, embrace your neck, and comfort you? Where are the daughters? When we think of these things, we realize that you are a lonely being, a pitiful and miserable being, one who cannot rely on anyone, as if you are in the late autumn season, in a place of despair where no one shows compassion, in a position where life and death are intertwined, and where you are in a place of deep sorrow and injustice. We come to understand that you are indeed such a father. There must be a group of people on this earth who claim to be your sons and daughters. 
We must know that we cannot approach you without tears. We must go with the dignity of being your children. 
Truly, there is a heart of the father who wants to command the children who understand your heart and will, and who are preparing to fulfill the mission given to them, and to find solutions in place of the position you are in. How pitiful and desperate it is to see humans who cannot fulfill this. 
"Oh, my child, what shall we do?" You must bear this burden and fight against the enemy to resolve it, and we must comfort you, the pitiful father who cannot find even one person on this earth to carry this burden. 
Is there a group on this earth that has vowed to establish the ideology of victory before you? Are there sons and daughters who are fighting at the forefront, carrying the cross in the world of the enemy to fulfill the unachieved will of heaven? There has been no such group in the historical era. Now, we know that the group capable of fulfilling this is the Unification group. When we realize that your wish is to be with them, and that the nation you desire cannot be without them, we come to feel how pitiful you are. 
How pitiful and miserable your situation must be, as you have entrusted this task to humans and have not been able to have a day of comfort or an hour of love. We know that there is such a past, and we recognize that such a present and possible future are approaching, so we must feel ashamed to reveal our faces before you. 
We must become those who can recognize that our thoughts of being sons and daughters are insufficient if we cannot approach you with the proper attitude. 
Father, please know our hearts and protect the path we must take. Please seek the nation we hope for. We know this is your goal and the path you must take. There must be something like a locomotive, something like coal, and there must be a driver. However, many have claimed to be the driver until now. Many have claimed to be the locomotive. But no one has claimed to be the coal. Today, we must be all three. 
How will we find ourselves to be the fuel that must be? We understand that children who are like sacrificial fuel are needed to move this earth. We must become a locomotive that knows the direction and serves as a purpose. We must become the driver. When we think about who will bear this burden, we must lay down tracks in this dark world of death and create a locomotive that can run on those tracks. We must also find the driver and produce the fuel. We already know that this is the mission of the Unification Church. 
Father, please be with us. We have come to understand that we must become the tracks, the fuel, the locomotive, and the driver. May we realize that this is the position where we can become one with you. We must know that you are seeking such a position. 
Father, how much effort have you put in to pave the way we must take in the world of death? How much effort have you put in to establish a Christianity that can run on the prepared tracks? Let us not forget that humanity's sacrifices and blood, sweat, and tears are intertwined in this. 
You have not forgotten this and have sent pioneers to move all of this. However, humans living on this earth have not been able to follow where they lead. We have understood that the tracks have diverged from the tracks, the drivers from the drivers, and the locomotives from the locomotives. Now, you have established a Unification Church that can unite this. Therefore, there must be tracks that you can follow within our Unification Church. There must be stored fuel. We must become a complete locomotive. We must become the driver. 
Thus, may we become a Unification Church that can move all religions and run vigorously toward the destination you desire. From this moment on, may we be your sons and daughters who run toward tomorrow's destination without stopping. 
Father, please remember Korea and Japan. Please connect them. Even today, there is a battle in the hearts of brothers who are not present here. Father, please protect them. Please remember them. Protect the path that Korea must take and the path we must take. 
We find ourselves in a position like captives. We know that to walk the path of destiny we must fight with both body and spirit. There is another path of destiny that we must pioneer, so please give us strength to walk this path. We sincerely ask for this. 
To do this, we have understood that we must overcome from the position of being sacrificial. May we be your children who can entrust everything to you, rely on you, do everything, and believe and follow you. 
Today is an unforgettable day. Because of that day in 1960, we were able to establish a new turning point in history, and we recognize that it became a day when we could overcome that turning point. We know that this day was an unforgettable historical turning point of suffering. How much effort have you put in from that time until today, which marks ten full years? Now, as we enter the latter half of the 1970s, Father, please protect us. 
We know that the fate of this nation is directly linked to the fate of Asia. No matter how strong the enemy is, we know the Father who has broken the enemy's limbs and prepared our path. Whether we believe in you this way or that way, may we realize that the only way for us to live is to act in unity with you, discussing and acting according to your will. 
Therefore, we must become one with you. We know that through us, you wish to find a family, a tribe, and a nation. We sincerely hope that none of your children who have fought until now will fall exhausted. 
May there be no pitiful group asking for salvation from the teacher of the Unification Church, and may we understand that as we walk this path, we must go along with you at every step. 
We must carry the heart of the parent and use the body of a servant, with blood, sweat, and tears, all...
For the sake of humanity and this universe, heaven and earth, we have come to the Unification Church to walk this path. Please help us understand from what point we started, what process we went through, and what results we must achieve. If we are deviating from the direction we should be heading, we sincerely hope and wish to be your children who can adjust our course and run towards a hopeful tomorrow.

In April, please allow us to make all the preparations we need, and we earnestly ask that you protect us as we march forward centered on the principles and truths. This year, Father, please watch over the path we must take centered on Asia towards the world.

Until that day comes, may we devote all our sincerity and loyalty to fulfill your will. Please remove the wrong things we possess and allow us to make progress solely centered on your will, so that we can leave only days of joy behind.

We know that there are still destinies of nations we must overcome until 1971, and we are aware that there are paths of destiny we must traverse. Therefore, Father, we earnestly ask for your protection.

From May, we will have to engage in new negotiations and prayers.

Father, please give us strength. Please unite our hearts. In the position of being the offering you desire, may we dedicate all our sincerity for the nation, and allow us to become sons and daughters who absolutely obey you in your deep heart.

Today is a holy day. Father, please be with your children who admire this place. Moreover, please remember our brothers scattered across South Korea, Japan, the United States, Germany, and all the children around the world, and allow them to be children who can feel your grace. I earnestly ask this in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> There is no day in life that is coincidental. Therefore, to meet a meaningful day, one must plan for that day in the morning and put that plan into action. To implement a plan, one must have an environment that aligns with one's intentions.

To lead a life of victory, the society, nation, and world we live in do not provide an environment that aligns with our intentions, which is why various hardships arise, and the crossroads of good and evil become intertwined. We know that no one can go in the direction we wish to go on our behalf. Every single person must struggle against their environment to lead their daily lives, and they must push through that environment. Thus, we feel keenly in our daily lives that no one can guarantee the success of the day's plans.

The more one feels that their environment is obstructing their daily life, and the larger that environment is—such as society or the world—the more determination and drive one must have to overcome that larger standard in order to achieve victory in their daily life. Without that, we cannot expect that day to be a day of victory.

Days accumulate to form a month, and months accumulate to form a year. When we look at a month, it consists of 30 days, right? However, that month does not have an environment that allows us to live as we planned. Therefore, to achieve victory in that month, we need the determination and drive to overcome all the complex circumstances and conditions that obstruct the path we planned.

Also, when we look at a year, it consists of twelve months and 365 days. If someone sets a goal for that year on New Year's Day, and if the conditions to overcome all trials and circumstances throughout that year do not align with them, then they will face resistance, opposition, and destructive environments. To push through that year, one must have the fighting spirit or drive to overcome more than 360 days. Without that, we know well that we cannot decorate the year with victory. 

This year adds up to ten years, twenty years, or thirty years, and we are walking that path in our lives. You must understand this.

Who can claim to be a victor? When we look at a year, there will be unavoidable difficulties. Living a life similar to that of a year, can anyone say, "I achieved victory like this"? We must recognize that no one has ever done so in history. Even sages and great figures, during their lives, stood as pioneers before humanity and achieved victory, or they achieved victory from a position of sacrifice. We know that no one has yet lived a life that embodies what all of humanity hopes for.

Considering that we have gone through such historical processes and that today we are entering such a historical era to weave that history, we must understand how difficult the life path we must fight through is. After we set our plans and vow to achieve victory, when we think of the sorrow of historical losers and the environments of historical incompleteness, we realize how shabby and pitiful our appearance is in reality.

If someone steps forward with a new resolution and new hope, saying, "I will go like this," history will inevitably mock them. It will ask, "Can you really do that? Can you achieve that?" In the face of such historical questions, we must ask ourselves if we can be confident over the course of a thousand years. Where can we find such a person in the human world? There has been none. Only the Absolute Being exists.

God, who still walks the path of the pioneer

Now, when we look at God's providence of restoration from the perspective of the Absolute Being, we must ask whether God has had a day of victory throughout the years, decades, or centuries of the providence of restoration. We know that God has not been able to escape the same fate as countless ancestors who have gone through historical destinies.

It is an enormous matter that we must inherit the fact that even the Absolute God has not established a point of victory in the historical era. 

Reflect on your own life. God has traversed a long period of 6,000 years. According to the Bible, it is 6,000 years, but it could correspond to millions or even hundreds of millions of years.

God has woven such a history until now. Has there ever been a day when God did not want to achieve victory? How much has God sought a day when He could fight against the enemy, break through their ranks, and lay the foundation for victory to rest? Yet, even now, He has not had that day and remains in a position where He must walk the path of struggle, the path of the pioneer. When we think of this, if someone today wishes to follow in His footsteps and inherit that mission, we must consider how much resolution and how many vows they must make.

Looking back at the past, a history of trials has been woven, and when we look at reality, a desolate world is sprawling widely. At this point, when we look toward the dark future, can anyone say, "God, please believe in me"? This is not a trivial matter. Yet, God cannot give up everything; He knows He has a responsibility to resolve this, so how will He break through this path?

From this perspective, we must understand that until now, God has never walked a day with joy. Why? Because He has walked with the sorrow of a loser. The first promise failed because of humanity, the second promise failed because of humanity, and through the third, fourth, and various historical eras, God has been in a position of repeated failures due to humanity.

Today, when we think of the fact that God cannot be in a position where He can confidently say, "I will achieve victory," we must recognize how pitiful God is, bearing the entire responsibility.

How can we know this? We can see it in our daily lives, in our yearly lives, and in our entire lives. God is leading countless humans who seek eternal life, so the pain of God as He moves toward the path of eternal life remains proportional to that pain. We cannot help but consider whether there is eternal pain and eternal sorrow interwoven in God as He seeks to find this.

God must bear an increasingly heavy cross

Now, when we consider our lives in relation to God, we must ask ourselves whether we are in a position of being a burden to God or whether we are in a position to take on God's burden. When we think about this, we find ourselves unable to escape the fate of being a burden to God even today. The more the number of burdens increases, the more sorrow will outweigh joy, won't it?

As the saying goes, "A tree with many branches has no day of rest," a parent with many children has no day of peace. How miserable must it be for God, who bears such responsibilities, as the number of burdens increases?

Today, our Unification Church has gone through ten years of history. In those ten years, there has been no smooth path. What remains in our memories are only the times we vowed in the valley of tears. What we remember are those times of tears, those times of sorrow and seriousness. Everything else has been forgotten. If there were a thousand people, there would have been serious times for each of them, but there would have been one day that was particularly serious. We remember that day. That day may be just one day for us, but for God, it may be a thousand days. When we consider this, we cannot help but acknowledge that as our numbers increase, the sorrow for God outweighs the joy.

As the number of individuals increases, their appearances become increasingly colorful. Different shapes emerge, and even if all of them come together to form one shape, that shape cannot be the embodiment of God's hope. To become that embodiment, either God must bear the heavy cross and walk the path of suffering, or humanity must do so. Without one side overcoming this, the joy of having many cannot manifest.

So who should take responsibility for this? Should God take responsibility, or should we? No matter how difficult it may be, God must take responsibility.

Why? Because God is in the position of a parent. No parent passes their burdens onto their children just because they are struggling. In the same way, the more difficult it gets for God, the more He will take responsibility. If He fails to fulfill that responsibility, God will lament over Himself. You must understand that God is in a position where He must strike Himself.

Today, when we face difficulties, we pray, "God, please take my burdens. I am walking the difficult path of a pioneer, so please take all my painful stories." We often pray like this, don't we? We must recognize that behind this prayer, God's sorrow is increasing.

When we think about this, you should feel how fearful it is to call out the name "Father." We must understand that within that word "Father," the stories of heaven and earth are intertwined. When we say, "Heavenly Father, be with us," we are asking God to bear thousands and thousands of crosses with us, to stand in the position of a servant for us, and to die for us. We must reflect on this.

A dutiful child before God

God has taken on the responsibility from a subjective position and has woven the history up to today, allowing us to reach a history like the one we have now. Since this history must move toward the future, it cannot remain stagnant at the present point. So, who will take responsibility for the path of the cross that God must walk today and in the future? If someone steps forward and says, "I will take responsibility," that person must take on God's responsibility.

We know that even overcoming the cross of one year is difficult, and we live experiencing countless grievances throughout a year. Yet, God has traversed the historical path of 6,000 years to save humanity. How many sad stories must have accumulated during that time, and how many lonely peaks must there have been? God is in a position of suffering that cannot be fathomed or imagined by humans.

You must understand this.

The more we think about this, the more fearful it is to pray. It is terrifying to call out the name "Father." When we realize that calling out to the Father while leaving behind the heavy cross is a shameful act, only then can God have hope in us. Instead of coming before God with confidence, saying, "God! I am proud, and I bear all responsibilities, so please protect me along with this responsibility," we should be a self who knows how to feel ashamed and worry about the inner cross we bear before God. 

When we cannot even convey our stories with our mouths and cannot reveal our appearances, we must recognize that the one word "Father," which slips out of our mouths after ten silent calls, is more precious than countless ordinary prayers.

Only in such a position will God say, "Even if you bear a cross, if it is your cross, I will take responsibility and resolve it." This is the only path where God can step forward. 

When we think about this, the path our Unification Church takes in relation to the will of the Father is the same. If we approach the Father with a bold attitude, saying, "Aren't you the beloved member of the Unification Church? Aren't you the beloved Unification Church?" then that position cannot be a place of hope where God can dwell. 

You must understand this.

Therefore, if you wish to take pride in the Unification Church, you must consider the Father who bears the heavy cross and approach from the position of fulfilling your duty as a child. To fulfill your duty of filial piety before a parent who works hard for you, you must first comfort your parent with tears and boldly carry the cross they bear. You must carry the path of the cross that you have walked, knowing that it was miserable for the sake of the children, and say, "Father, please do not suffer any longer."
Father, please do not worry about me any longer. I must stand in a position where I can do something. Is this not the appearance of a filial son who can stand before God, who has come out while suffering until now? When I think of this, I realize that today we have been so shameless and so arrogant before God.

Arrogant humans before God
You must understand that this position of arrogance and self-assurance we have today is still a place where we cannot go alongside God. Before God, who looks at me, there remains a chasm that must be filled between the Father and me. To become a citizen of that kingdom, we must endure trials and pains once again; this path of pioneers remains for us to walk.

God has repeatedly fulfilled the mission of a pioneer in the history of restoration more than any pioneer in the world, a fact that no one in the human world may know today. You may come to know this fact when you go to the spirit world, but in reality, it cannot be known.

Therefore, if there is anyone on this earth who claims to take responsibility for the world or history and to be an example for others, they must be seen as a foolish person. They should be the ones to tell others to emulate God rather than themselves.

Jesus also knew this fact, which is why he could say, "Father, not my will, but Yours be done." Here, my will is the desire to return immediately to the Father centered on the nation of Israel, but the Father's will is that to turn this around, He must walk the path of the cross. Knowing this, if there is a foundation of comfort where one can solve it by investing oneself due to the concern for God, then the place where one resolved to go, even if it meant tearing oneself apart and disappearing on the cross, was the Garden of Gethsemane.

Today, in any nation on this earth, there is a pioneer who has paved the way for that nation, and in any region, there is a pioneer who has paved the way for that region. However, while it may seem that humans have taken the initiative in pioneering something, you must understand that there is nothing that does not involve God behind it.

Everything in the world must be under God's dominion, and history must be so, and the times must be so. Therefore, those who claim to advocate new things that can remain in the times and history are pioneers in that field of that era, but you must know that behind the emergence of that pioneer, God has repeatedly traversed the path of the pioneer.

You must understand that God, who has pioneered a thousand times, hesitates to present even once. If a foundation of victory built through a thousand efforts is presented incorrectly even once, everything that was built through a thousand efforts can collapse in an instant, and to restore this, one must retrace the path of the pioneer multiplied by thousands of times. Therefore, to entrust one task on this earth for pioneering, the path of the cross, which has been multiplied countless times, must be laid before God. Because of this, we must understand that God has walked this path of the pioneer until now.

When you stand in the position of a pioneer or a seer, you must not think that you have stood there by yourself. You must know that before you stand in that position, God has stood there hundreds of millions of times. Before I stand in the position of a pioneer, God has stood in the position of a pioneer hundreds of millions of times, and before I stand in the position of a seer, God has stood in the position of a seer hundreds of millions of times.

However, there is a God who has never been able to boast of having won as a pioneer on any given day, and there is a God who has fought while narrowing the scale before a new era from the position of a seer but has never been able to boast. When we think of such a God from the perspective of a seer, we must recognize that the fallen humans of today are far too arrogant.

Endurance and overcoming
A pioneer cannot walk that path without patience. Today, this very moment requires adventure, and everything that collides there is unfamiliar and requires new efforts.

Today, when we consider history and culture, there are cases where a nation or people is praised as a cultural nation. When we look at the relics or remains left by such a nation, we realize that they were achieved through countless adventures and created from overcoming numerous difficulties.

In the same way, how immense must God's path be in pioneering the path of human salvation to establish a cultural realm in the historical age? We must understand that God's position in pioneering that path could not be walked without indescribable patience and overcoming suffering. How much must one endure on that path? Even if there are successive crises of death, this is the path that God has walked, and you must understand this.

If there were no enemies, one might not know, but the fact that there are enemies attacking means that at any moment, God could suffer a sudden collapse of the thousand-year work due to an enemy's assault. You must understand that God is present on this path, overcoming the way of suffering with such a tense heart, while enemies are holding swords and aiming arrows.

Indeed, even at the moment when God is looking forward to a glimmer of hope to distinguish between black and white from a position of exhaustion, enemies are aiming their weapons at God. In such a weary position, where one would want to rest, one must face the enemy and make the final decision; has there ever been a day when God could relax and feel at ease? Therefore, we must recognize that God is pitiful.

Endurance and overcoming are everything in His life, and sacrifice is everything in His life. That struggle is not a habitual or historically repetitive struggle; rather, as the scope broadens, the struggle becomes increasingly complex and widespread.

You must think about how difficult it must be for God, who has come through such a historical era. When it is night in the East and people are resting, it is daytime in the West. While Eastern people are resting at night, there will be some Western people praying to God, and there will be those who are fighting centered on God. Can God, looking at this earth, rest for even a moment in 24 hours? When we see that the affairs of this world cannot be resolved without God, God is in a position where He must be involved in everything from one thing to ten million things and must make decisions of goodness.

Therefore, God must be an exceedingly pitiful being. When we think about this, the question arises: how many times have you had moments in your faith life where you wanted to pray about complicated issues centered on yourself but could not pray and instead shed tears?

The sons and daughters that God desires
The difficulties I face are hardships for God, so please return the price of those hardships to my sons and daughters. I work hard for the Unification Church, so please return the price of that hard work to the Unification Church! Many people believe and work from this standpoint, but how many truly embrace God's inner heart and overcome the path of suffering? Is it not the case that the current state of God, who has sustained history while bearing the adversities of struggle, is one that should not lose hope for tomorrow?

How much of a life of adversity has God lived while carrying this heavy and difficult cross? However, the reason He cannot give this up is that the heart of a parent who must find lost sons and daughters remains. Because He is omniscient and omnipotent, the only way He can take responsibility is through the path of restoration.

A limited person in a limited era cannot even dream of taking responsibility for this through their lifetime. This work can only be fully responsible by God Himself from the beginning to the end of history because He alone is omniscient and omnipotent; no human can take responsibility for it. This is the path of restoration that God knows.

The problem here is that it is miserable and pitiful that humans live their lives without realizing that they are in the position of such a God and cannot help but live a life that increases the cross before God. Then, why has this pity arisen? It arose because of the fall of the human ancestors. Therefore, what I must overcome is how to eradicate the elements of evil that can invade centered on goodness.

Living is not about living well. Even if one cannot live well, the very act of not leaving behind one's cross before God can be a form of filial piety before Him. Countless people who come and go on this earth leave behind the path of the cross that has been multiplied before God in their lives, but I will not leave my cross behind before God, no matter how much I walk the path of suffering or face difficult adversities. I will take responsibility for my own burdens. This is what God wants to see in His sons and daughters.

Even if my cross is mine, I will not leave it before God and will take responsibility for it. If there are sons and daughters who say this and act accordingly, God will call them filial children. Furthermore, the burden you bear is a burden for humanity, a burden that our ancestors wrongly bore, and if there is someone who says they will take responsibility for that burden, even if that person cannot fulfill that task and cannot be held accountable, God's inner heart would want to speak to them about the historical significance of that matter.

Today, we must shed the naive faith path of our past and move away from the habitual or customary faith perspective centered on God that we have had since before 1960. In the 1970s, we must at least maintain our dignity and become individuals who do not leave behind our crosses before God, and we must become the Unification Church. Even if we take responsibility for just this, God will commend us for fulfilling the mission of a pioneer that no one has done or could bear in the course of human history until now. You must understand that this is God's heart.

I am responsible for two crosses
Here, we have learned that God has borne all the crosses of the historical process. This is not because God has made mistakes, but because humanity has made mistakes. That humanity is our ancestors, and they are related to us. I was born as the totality of that relationship. Ultimately, if there are those who sincerely bear all the historical responsibilities that God has borne on their behalf, what kind of prayer should they first offer? They must offer prayers of repentance. They must become those who can resolve the erroneous history passed down from their ancestors. They must comfort God, who has been filled with regret for not being able to settle the valleys filled with tears and sweat, with tears of repentance. Without having such a moment, one cannot claim to have fulfilled their responsibilities before God in the real world.

Therefore, today, we Unification Church members must repent not centered on ourselves but centered on history. Because Unification Church members have taken responsibility for history, they must repent for history, and because they have taken responsibility for the present age, they must repent for this age. Because they stand in the position of representing all humanity in the past and present, they must stand in the position of being a sacrificial offering.

This position is a sorrowful position that represents countless ancestors who have repeatedly failed in history and the current 3 billion people who are repeating the history of failure. Therefore, if there is someone who understands this situation and can pioneer even a thread of comfort before God, allowing a connection to be made on this earth or in the historical age, then those living in this era should be grateful to that person, and countless prophets and sages who have come and gone in the historical age must also be grateful to them.

Then, when will you leave behind such a moment in your life? The question of whether you can leave behind such a moment through your life or not is a significant issue that we who are currently living a faith life must resolve. In this regard, am I a betrayer of history or a leader of history? Am I a betrayer of the times or a leader of the times? When we think about this, God has fought to lead history and has fought to lead the times. To receive support from God, I must first have a moment of support from history and a moment of support from the times. Without having such a pivotal moment, I cannot stand before God.

Such a position is not a place where one shows themselves because they have made such and such a resolution and are in such and such a position. That is only a moment, a fleeting time. The faith path is to extend that moment over a year, to extend that year over ten years, and to walk a lifetime to connect those ten years. The issue is how to connect that moment of victory in a day to a year, that year to ten years, and that ten years to a lifetime. You must understand that the path of a believer is to solidify the heart and spirit and move forward.

In a position of self-centered self-blame, the faith path cannot be established. No matter how much difficulty comes upon me, I must not avoid it. If I try to escape the cross that comes upon me, a double cross will remain. Why is that? It is because I am a product of history and a product of the times; the burdens that the ancestors of the past could not bear are being multiplied upon me, and the burdens that the current age cannot bear are being multiplied upon me. In this way, I am bearing two burdens.

If I try to avoid that cross, it results in returning the historical cross and the cross of the times that were inherited to God. Thus, the game of carrying a double cross is becoming our faith path today.

In this way, since I exist to support history and the times, I must understand that I am in a position to indemnify history and indemnify the times. Because of this relationship, the history of the Second Advent is possible. Reality bears a dual historical nature; therefore, victories in reality can bring about historical victories, and failures in reality can bring about historical failures. Thus, we must understand that if we evade responsibility, we will burden God with the double cross we bear.

This is a fact that we must not return to God, and it is a fact that must not be allowed to happen to God. You must think about how that becomes a true tragedy for parents and fight to prevent this in your lifetime. This is the faith path we must walk today.

A correct attitude towards God
So, how should we, who are in such a position, face God?

We know this through the principles.

Many people have labored according to the will of providence for this, and God has also labored for it. Even if I realize that I am not such a self, and I criticize past people for how one should live, and even if I can present a new purpose and direction to current humanity, I still cannot become a self that can boast of myself. 

Why is that? What should humans boast about? It is absurd to boast about one's good looks externally. Also, to think that being the object of admiration for a few people in a specific environment is enough to boast before the history of restoration or before heaven is impossible. 

This is because we have lost the most precious thing that we can boast about. So even if I know the direction I should go, it does not end with just knowing; I must go the way I should go as a human. Only then can my value be eternally recognized by heaven and earth, or I can be drawn into that value. We must reach a level where we can do that. When we consider what can be the content of such value, all external appearances and all connections related to the environment cannot be something to boast about. These are too far removed from that value. 

What kind of savior do humans desire? 
Then, what possesses such precious value is someone who can save the poor self in a difficult position. That is why I long for such a person. Also, those who have believed in religion until now have longed for a central being, a Messiah or Savior, who can save their lives, possessions, and all other connections. No. We will demand a savior who can stand in a position where we can have a deeper relationship than that. In other words, we will seek a savior who can be closer to us than a relative or a brother. From this perspective, when we consider what kind of value we hope our savior will manifest, we can understand that the ultimate destination humans seek is their parents. There is nothing more precious than parents. Parents are the mother and father. However, when I am in a position of suffering, I need a way, and to overcome all harsh circumstances, I need parents, and we come to realize that we need the father more than the mother. There may be someone who calls for the mother, but in such situations, it is generally the father who is called. 

But what if one's own parents cannot save them? They will call upon God. Throughout the historical process, what could humanity express as a final testament with a heart of seeking salvation? It is the words, "Father! God!" There is no need for anything more than this. 

We are in such a position, yet we live without realizing that we are in such a position. I offer my remaining life before You, and I hope that You will directly lead my descendants to the kingdom of freedom where they can be embraced by You. I entrust all that we have to You. I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.

A person with good ancestors must sacrifice.
