6) Solid Foundation
<Prayer> Father, during the course of restoration, countless of your children have been sacrificed. How much have you fought along with the times, and how many people have you suffered for? The more I think about the long years you have left behind sorrow and resentment, the more I feel that we, who have nothing, must be even more faithful to the mission of the remaining blessing. 

Father, all things in this world were created through your effort and grace, but due to the fall of humanity, all these things remain as points of sorrow for you. I earnestly hope and wish that you will make us feel this fact deeply. 

In the midst of such sorrow, we recognize that the world, the nation, the people, the race, the family, and the individual we live in are all in this state. 

We cannot show our faces or maintain our dignity before the efforts of the Father who created the world for the sake of one individual. If you were to ask us how much of a personality we have become, we would not be able to show our faces or maintain our dignity. The more we discover this state, the more we realize that the only one who is pitiful is the Father. 

Today is the Sabbath. Please remember your children scattered throughout the nation and the many children around the world. 

As the final battle approaches us, grant us the understanding that it is time to align our steps and form ranks to conclude the final contest. Make me someone who can do this both internally and externally. Let us realize that you are earnestly waiting for children who are capable of fulfilling this tremendous mission. 

Father, we must give our all to fulfill the great providential purpose we are planning this year. May the time come soon when we can proudly raise the flag of victory, having dedicated our inadequate selves to the holy sanctuary, and proclaim that the entire universe has been liberated. 

Father, do not regard our circumstances and situations. We do not possess anything that you can trust. We should know your circumstances, but we have not yet understood them. However, we know that to reach that position, we must overcome countless trials and hardships, so please do not let us become weary in this battlefield. And as we receive your protection on the front lines, may we be your children who are busy marching and mobilizing toward the final battleground. 

Please grant ten thousand blessings upon the countless children of yours who are scattered across South Korea, looking toward this place, worshiping, and hoping for heavenly grace. Also, please extend your deep protective hand to the children of unity who are devoted to your providential purpose around the world. I earnestly hope and wish that you will always protect them when they are in difficulty or loneliness. 

This year, we must achieve a goal that surpasses the national ideal. After establishing Japan to protect the nation, if you spread your hand of blessing there and made them fight, may the glory of the victory they achieve in the end be within your glory, and may we have a day to praise that victory. 

Thus, may the children of unity be able to rise up with your will in Asia, and may the day come soon when we can boast that we could win because your providential purpose was such. 

On this day, wherever we gather and call upon your name, please bestow your holy grace, and through them, expand the foundation of your victory so that the children of unity can inherit it. 

May we understand the deep will of the Father who comes not for the individual but for the whole. 

I earnestly ask you to personally oversee everything from this moment on, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

<Word> People living on earth are seeking something better. The reason people demand something good is that it possesses greater value and, at the same time, greater eternity. 

What is most needed in the providence of restoration?
People want to become better. This is because their individual entities can possess something that can remain with the past, present, and future. In other words, a good person stands on a solid foundation that no one can invade, which is why humans pursue becoming good people. 

We know that evil does not last long. Evil only stands against for a moment. It also does not possess the content that can establish history beyond the era. History is continuous over eternity, and the motivation to sustain it is momentary. However, because an eternal history cannot be achieved through an evil process, we humans do not like evil people or evil things. 

Just as we humans desire good things, we must understand that God also desires good things. This is because, just as humans need an unchanging solid foundation or firm base in their lives, this is also necessary in the face of the will of the providence of restoration. 

So, what is the first thing needed in the face of the providence of restoration? We must understand that a person standing on a foundation more solid than any external material is needed. Therefore, we humans must first become important people before pursuing material. So, what kind of person is that? It is a person who can stand on an unchanging solid foundation in the course of restoration history. It is through such people that history began and has moved until now. No matter how well external conditions are prepared, without such people, those conditions cannot become a good foundation, cannot be used for good purposes, cannot achieve good purposes, and cannot remain in good places. Considering these facts, we must recognize that the person is the problem in carrying out the providence of restoration. 

Just as a person is central to establishing a solid foundation for a household, it is the same in the providence of restoration. A nation is also formed and maintained by people. If those people have a national perspective that aligns with the purpose of the whole rather than individual purposes, that nation can develop infinitely. Therefore, we must recognize that a person standing on an unchanging solid foundation is more precious than anything else for those of us who pursue goodness. 

The value of a person standing on a solid foundation
When we focus on a person, we observe their words, actions, and mindset. We see whether their words, actions, and mindset are standing on a solid foundation. Therefore, a person must stand on a completely solid and unchanging foundation. A person who changes according to the time and environment cannot influence the nation, the people, the family, or individuals. Here, we feel how important the actions, mindset, and words of a person standing on a solid foundation are. 

When a person is called a person of character, the words and actions that appear in the character of that person are done on a solid foundation, so no one can move them. Even if it is a friend, or someone in a position of power, or even someone very close, when they speak words that cannot be moved, new connections arise from there, and everything begins from that point. 

The same goes for actions. When actions are taken from an unchanging solid position, even if those actions are temporary, they can move history and represent the era. 

When the number of such individuals increases and manifests as one action, it can become a movement that can transform a nation and also a source that can establish a new nation. Therefore, if there are tribes formed by individuals standing on a solid foundation, that tribe or nation will not start and stop within a limited timeframe, but will begin from a position that transcends that timeframe and extend toward eternity. Considering this fact, we must reflect on how much we have pursued such individuals at this point in time. 

The person that God needs
We say that although God has been carrying out the providence of restoration for 6,000 years, He has not yet found one man and one woman. Until now, there have been many men and women in this world, and many couples. There have also been forms of nations and countries. However, there has not been a single person who can receive and respond to God's eternal and unchanging word, nor has there been anyone who can inherit and perpetuate God's eternal work. This is the sorrow of God that we must understand. 

In any family, if it is a family with a name that can move history and has the traditions of a nation, how great would the sorrow be if there are no children who can inherit such things? If there are children in that family, everything established in that family will shine even more. And all connections related to that family will also shine. However, if there are no children who can inherit the deep content of that family, that family will begin to decline from there. 

God's will is similar to our environmental content. If there is a true person who can inherit the eternal will centered on God, there is nothing lacking in starting toward future glory, but when such a person does not exist, no matter how solid a position God may be in, He will inevitably be powerless before humanity and history, and cannot pass on all of God's works. Therefore, we cannot help but think about how precious a human being standing on a solid foundation is. That is why God has been striving to find such individuals until now. 

So, today, I myself am in the face of the will that God is seeking.
Have you taken such a firm position? This is a significant issue that we must reconsider.  
God must have individuals who are steadfast and can align with His will. When this is not the case, no matter how great the will is or how opportune the time may seem to fulfill that will, both the will and the timing become useless. In that sense, we must reflect on whether each of us, as members of the Unification Church who bear a historical mission today, has truly become someone who cannot be changed by anyone trying to alter them, nor can they be modified, and whether we have become complete beings who do not need any additional support. If such a person exists here, they must be a source of joy for God and the center of hope for countless people today.  
When such a person appears on this earth, humanity will finally start from a solid foundation before the providence of restoration. Therefore, the question is when you will stand on such a standard and when you will take such a position.  
When an individual stands in such a position, they will have the content that can serve as a motive to represent history, and that history will be able to inherit it. Furthermore, when they carry out practical measures along with that motive, new results of practice will emerge in history. Considering all these issues, you must understand how necessary it is to have individuals standing on a firm foundation.  
Unification Church members must stand on a solid foundation  
Today, you are representatives of thirty million people. Whether you are men or women representing this entire nation, how much have you longed to stand on a foundation where you can represent this entire people? In loving the thirty million, you should not take any intermediate position but should stand on a solid foundation, that is, on a point where God can start. Thus, you must declare that you will take responsibility and fight for the thirty million. Such individuals are needed in the will.  
When such people connect and form families, and those families connect to form tribes, and those tribes connect to form one nation, through that nation, a new world will finally unfold vigorously in accordance with God's will. In light of this issue, you must feel how necessary it is to have a self that stands on a solid foundation.  
When we look at the four thousand years of history leading up to Jesus, centered on God's providential will, that history was a tumultuous one. It was a history that could not find a certain point of settlement. Because it could not become a solid foundation as a rock, humanity could not stand on it, and as a result, everything that acted could not become a new approach before history, nor could it stand on a foundation that could influence that era.  
From that perspective, the one who came to fulfill that mission is Jesus. However, Jesus' mission has been extended to this day, two thousand years later. Therefore, there are groups that feel a sense of responsibility to once again take up that mission centered on the Republic of Korea. How serious must that group be?  
Today, the world situation is tumultuous. The fate of nations is also in turmoil. If individuals, families, or tribes capable of managing the nations and the world in such a situation can emerge, it is from there that a new world will be established. You must understand this.  
Therefore, we must become individuals who can do so. God desires such individuals, and His will cannot be fulfilled without us. Thus, if there is someone who can fulfill that will, God will certainly anchor Himself to that person. God will seek the motivation for stagnation or initiation from that foundation. In light of this, we must stand on a solid foundation. We must become individuals, families, and tribes that stand on a solid foundation.  
Then, what kind of group should become such a tribe? It should be us, the members of the Unification Church today. We must also become a nation that stands on such a foundation, and that nation should be the Republic of Korea, which must fulfill the mission of the Third Israel. This is the problem.  
To achieve this, we must start from individuals standing on a solid foundation. To become such individuals,  
what I do must be certain actions, and what I say must be certain words. Therefore, my words and actions represent history, and only by believing my words and following my actions can all historical issues be resolved and determined.  
We must become individuals standing on a belief that can do so.  
Words spoken from such a position should not be temporary words but should be words that can continue until the entire Republic of Korea can achieve that result. The same goes for actions. In the process of moving forward, no matter how difficult the problems may be, they do not become issues for us who stand on a solid foundation.  
We must stand in a position to move forward.  
Therefore, if our Unification Church also moves forward from this position, no matter how difficult the path we take may be, it does not become a problem. As long as that difficulty is not beyond the solid foundation we stand on, we will not yield and can surely pledge the results of victory. You must understand that this issue is resolved through each of our responsibilities.  
Jesus advised the weak in faith to believe, saying, "For those who believe, nothing will be impossible." Here, the call to believe is not a vague belief. It means to stand on a solid foundation and a rock and not to be shaken. It means not to stand in a position influenced by anyone's interference or invasion from that foundation.  
To stand on a solid foundation,  
God always hopes that we will establish our own subjectivity and leading authority. God emphasizes absolute faith in those who are in a vague position because He needs an absolutely solid foundation, even if only temporarily. Therefore, we must understand how pitiful God is.  
God is in a position to lead all beings and the entire universe toward one purpose on an eternal foundation. However, having lost that subjective position, He has become a God who seeks to unfold the providential will from a position that establishes relative standards through makeshift measures. Therefore, we must reconsider how pitiful God is.  
This is why we need principles. We need principles and rules. These principles and rules cannot be interfered with by anyone. They are not within the realm of history but are at a point that transcends history and can move history. They are not in the position of historical results. Therefore, principles cannot be interfered with by any ancestors or descendants. Both ancestors and descendants must comply with them. Moreover, history must also comply. Because the principle itself is a principled content with absolute subjectivity, our Unification Church advocates the principle.  
The path of the principle is a path that advocates and goes to illuminate, expand, and reveal the solid foundation. You must understand this point. Therefore, the path of the principle is not an easy path to traverse. It is not a path that can be easily stepped over by any means or methods. The path of the principle is a path that must be stepped over one by one.  
If ten people go, they must all go in the same manner. Otherwise, it cannot be said that they have traveled this path. Even if a hundred people go, if they do not all go in the same manner, it cannot be said that they have traveled this path, and even if ten million people go, they must all go through the same path.  
The path of the principle means that even if it is a distance of ten steps, it must leave a form that transcends history. Here, neither our ancestors nor our descendants can be altered, and even God cannot be altered. You must understand that this is the path of the principle.  
However, the path of indemnity is different. If it is one-tenth, it can be indemnified with a conditional form, whether it is one-tenth or one-hundredth. We understand that this is the path of indemnity and restoration.  
However, what we need is not indemnity and restoration, but the principle above all. Only with this principle can the historical origin emerge, and only when we are based on this principle can we stand on a solid foundation. Therefore, how much we reveal the self that stands on this foundation becomes a matter of how much we live in accordance with the principle.  
When we look at the members of our Unification Church or the special blessing trainees this time, the standard for evaluating them is not how long they have lived after knowing the will, even if that period is shorter than the past, but how much they have lived in accordance with the principled content after knowing the will.  
Thus, whether it has been one hour, one year, three years, or ten years since entering the Unification Church, the question is how much they have stood on a principled position and a solid foundation. This will shine a light on the value of their lives and can determine the issues of their lives in the future.  
Why is that? It is because by serving under the principled standard, one can be closer to the absolute standard. When the living standard aligns with the principle, from there, that life aligns with the eternal will, and the issues of eternal life are determined by the content that aligns with that standard. This is because living centered on the principle becomes God's solid foundation.  
Therefore, living apart from the principle is extremely dangerous. However, when we live based on the principle and in harmony with it, a solid and firm foundation will remain in our life journey. Thus, we must speak with the principle, live with the principle, and practice with the principle. Only through that can we awaken history, lead history, and establish a new era.  
We must live a thorough principled life  
You must understand that if you do not engage in internal or external life, or economic or faith life on this foundation, you cannot have a stable life. A principled life from such a position can influence even our life and death issues. Such a life in this world will not only remain in the present but will also become a foundation that lasts into the eternal world. You must know that this is the principle that the Unification Church advocates, and you must live based on this principle. We must remember that all the goals we seek in our lives will become a solid foundation that can last forever, starting from a life that aligns with the principle.  
Those who live while contemplating and investing in that content cannot tire out. When God acts together with those who live this way, it can become a more solid foundation and a motive for creating a new history tomorrow. Therefore, if we continue such a life, we must know that it will become the origin of our horizontal and vertical development and strive even more.  
This is the position that our Unification Church members should take at present.  
You must be aware that the current situation in Korea is heading toward a critical point. Then, how will this point be changed, and by whose power? It cannot be changed by any national policy. It can only be changed depending on how many people with a firm belief that can connect the fate of the nation to the fate of the world exist among that people.  
This will become the motive to save the urgent fate of the country.  
At this current point, you must realize how important the attitude and position of our Unification Church believers living according to the principles of the Unification Church are. We know well that there is no other source or foundation that can gather all the people of the world, not just the Republic of Korea. It must be achieved within the realm of our lives centered on the principle.  
From this perspective, we must feel how solemn and tremendous the position we are in is. You must understand that the solid foundation that our individuals must establish, the solid foundation that families must establish, and the solid foundation that nations and tribes must establish all start from the principle. Therefore, I believe we must emphasize the thoroughness of principled living even more.

If there is no entity on this earth that can embody such content, this world will rot like dead fruit. In autumn, there is no significant difference between the appearance of dead fruit and the appearance of fruit with vitality. Externally, it is not apparent. Others may not know, but the essence knows. Therefore, one must recognize whether they are dead or alive.

When we look at the world today, when spring arrives in the tropics, it will also come to the northern regions...
will be welcomed. In places where the temperature exceeds 23 degrees, autumn days will come. This means that the forms of spring, summer, autumn, and winter are unfolding on this planet. In today's human history, to greet a globally boundless spring day, we must personally connect spring, summer, and autumn in succession. Without doing so, we cannot welcome a new spring day. 

To prepare for the historical spring season that will come again after the end, we need to possess the vitality that can connect with the spring, the vitality that can connect with the summer, the vitality that can connect with the autumn, and the vitality that can overcome winter. The essence of having such vitality must encompass the connections of spring, summer, autumn, and winter. Even if there is one person who possesses all of that, it cannot be welcomed as spring globally at once, so God has worked through individuals in the context of the long historical process for the 3 billion people of the world, and you must understand that there was a time when God worked the grace of the spring season through individuals. 

Even if it is an individual, there must be someone who connects that vitality and does not lose the connection with the summer season from within, and who can establish a relationship with God. Additionally, among those connected to the summer season, there must be at least one person who can represent the entire universe with the vitality of the autumn season. Thus, there must be at least one person with whom God is present, who can emerge on earth with new vitality. However, since the entity that is to emerge is fallen humanity, that entity cannot be one with vitality. Therefore, God must be the foundation of life. This is why the concept of the Messiah exists before humanity.

So, who is the Messiah? Is he not the one who brings the cultural content of the spring season that humanity should have? Is he not a global figure who brings the content and worldview of a civilization that can develop infinitely and prosper infinitely like the summer season? Is he not someone who can inform us of the fruits of the autumn season and can represent that value on a global scale, not just personally? Beyond that, we must think that there has been God's inner providence to overcome the winter season and to prepare for a global spring day by overcoming the insufficiencies of the world. However, today, if there is someone like the Messiah among us humans, who are groping in the darkness of the fallen realm, what guest could be more worthy of our joyful welcome? 

That is why, in the midst of the current global crisis facing humanity, we are seeking a new global leader. This itself is humanity indirectly pursuing the concept of the Messiah, is it not? 

The fairness of the seasons that humanity is born into
In spring, there are various flowers, various types of trees, and countless kinds of plants. Seeing this is likely similar to how God sees us humans. When we observe these things, when the spring season returns, how can we not welcome spring, and where is there anything that does not possess life? From the smallest insect to a blade of grass, a large tree, all flying birds, and even humanity, all created beings are living with the connections of life. We cannot deny the fact that all these created beings start with a connection in the spring season. 

From this perspective, a spring day will come to our world today. In welcoming that spring day, what kind of tree will I become in that spring garden? You are in a position of individuality. Therefore, some may become a blade of grass, while others may become a certain tree. In this way, there will be individuals, tribes, and nations that possess life in various fields of different kinds. There will be individuals and nations symbolizing integrity, like the pine and bamboo, and there will be individuals, families, tribes, and nations that can encompass all connections like flowers. 

The connections of the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter have been intertwined since the beginning of historical times. The fate of your life is similarly intertwined and cyclical. We must consider why some people live well while others do not from this perspective. 

The reason some people live well is that their ancestors have already gone through the winter season. They are living well because they have entered the realm where they can welcome the spring season. Likewise, why are some people flourishing? It is because they have laid the foundation of the spring season that can welcome the summer season. When one flourishes, they will inevitably bear fruit. Everything that cools will inevitably tilt, thus welcoming the autumn season. 

However, individuals or nations that despair or lose hope upon welcoming the autumn season will perish. You must understand this. If you despair just because you have welcomed the autumn season, you will perish. Those who start from the autumn season will naturally wither as they go on. Yet, those who sigh, saying, "Oh, we have been punished. What a twist of fate!" are pitiful people. If you have welcomed the autumn season, you must possess the vitality to overcome the approaching winter season. No matter how harsh the trials may be, we must go on with a belief that we can overcome and pioneer through that winter season. If there is a nation that can overcome the winter season, it can welcome the spring season that comes again. 

From this perspective, you are on a path of fate that cannot escape the continuous connections of the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter in the historical age. You must understand that your own life was born within such connections, and thus you are the embodiment of fate. However, among people, there are those born in spring and those who unfortunately were born in winter. In other words, there are those who were born as the sons of wealthy families or kings, enjoying all glory in the summer season. There are also those born in the autumn season. You must understand this. Upon reflection, the history of this universe is fair. 

Being born in the winter season is not a bad thing. Even if one is born in winter, if they advance vigorously without being harmed in any way, they will see the arrival of spring faster than anyone else. They will grow stronger than anyone else. 

To overcome the winter season
So, what should the members of our Unification Church compare the capabilities they possess within themselves to? You have likely felt the peak of the sorrow of the fallen realm, the world of sad culture, and the world of prideful lamentation, and you have also felt the despair of a withering culture that has encountered a desperate environment. However, none of that should dominate me. No season should dominate me. You must become the kind of person who can say this. Therefore, you must discover yourself as a being who can connect the seasons with vitality and become the embodiment of life that can smoothly overcome winter. A person with such a worldview will not perish even if history perishes, that era perishes, and the world perishes. Thus, the issue is becoming such a person. 

We have been on the path to becoming such a person until now. Whether in the path where our nation persecutes us, in the terrible environment where our tribe opposes us, or in the environment where other nations wield swords and push us into the peak of suffering, we have come this far. Therefore, even if loneliness strikes and the realm of lamentation swirls around me, we must not become those who try to escape that realm. 

The closer we get to the end times, the more we must face it head-on. We must break through it. We must determine whether you will break or I will break. Here, we must possess the vitality that can shed a layer and become a foundation that brings hope for tomorrow. The belief that can praise the fruitful self with such vitality is what matters. 

By establishing such a self, you must be able to confidently say, "I am a dignified self who can welcome spring." Thus, by welcoming spring and making it your foundation, you must have the authority to develop infinitely, so that you can bring all people together into fruition. 

When one seed is sown, there is a harvest of 30-fold, 60-fold, or 100-fold. Similarly, when you sow one on this earth, the result must bear fruit, even if it is one in ten million. Humanity must see that and be able to pledge victory for tomorrow. The more the number of those who can boldly take responsibility for the winter season of suffering increases, the more the world will welcome the new spring day of resurrection. 

From this standpoint, if there is a great person who looks forward with strength and marches forward, history will turn back from here. You must also understand that the moment when the path of fate, which flows eternally into the winter season and falls into the realm of death, can be transformed into a new spring season begins from here. 

We often say that we are the historical fruits. O Heaven! We declare that we are the fruits of six thousand years of history. Then, have you become a being with the vitality to overcome the winter season, which is the culmination of the trials accumulated over six thousand years of historical process? This is the issue. You must understand that this is a decisive factor that can determine your victory or defeat. 

Before the new world cultural history, like the spring season that comes at the end, I must open the door of my heart wide. In this way, in the garden where I have opened all my arms, the world’s humanity can bloom infinitely and can praise the privileged self that can govern infinitely. When that happens, you can advance to the position of the highest human being that the original humanity desired. 

If God loves humanity, He must have created us as beings of such value. We are not beings created to sigh and despair, placed at the final edge of fate like today. For the sake of a tomorrow that can express such existential value, to discover such a self, and to develop such an unknown self, we must understand that we have entered this path today. 

In the path I walk, I must be able to welcome a tomorrow where individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world can collide head-on before me. Our church has come this far to meet such a time. We have been able to bear much fruit among this, but many have also fallen away. 

Overcoming trials and bearing fruit
We must be able to say that now is better than the spring season, summer season, or autumn season of human history. Only then can life be unleashed. You must understand that a new start of joy must arise from the deep peak and boundary of the winter season for spring to come normally. 

Looking at the history of Israel, there were always trials before the grace came. That is why spring is called the season of grace. Before welcoming spring, we must think about the past that has allowed spring to come. Therefore, we must welcome spring while longing for the historical connection of life in this spring season. Additionally, spring is to seek a valuable seed of life that can connect the cosmic connections of the summer and autumn seasons that we must welcome tomorrow. This is the start of spring. 

When we look at the many kinds of flowers welcoming the start of spring, we must resolve to overcome the difficulties of the autumn season that comes after summer and pursue fruition. If you do not remain as a self who can make such a judgment, you will not be able to welcome the hopeful spring season that humanity will collectively pursue in the future. 

So, have you truly welcomed the spring day, the summer, the autumn day, and the winter day from the position of knowing God's will centered around this age of grace? 

When grace like spring comes, everyone wants to give everything. They want to befriend everyone. Then, when summer comes, they become lush around their own entity. For example, if the spring season is the time when barley leaves become lush, then the summer season is the time when the stalk grows. The purpose of the lush leaves is to establish one stalk, and barley that does not produce that stalk in the summer season will not bear fruit. 

And within that stalk, new changes must occur. One must become a position that can be praised before all things in place of their own beauty, like a flower. At the same time, one must become an embodiment of fruition. On that foundation of the heart, one must absorb the continuous essence of life in the process centered around the autumn season after going through the summer season. Therefore, you should not suffer losses from everything that passes through and collides with you; rather, you should add the essence of life. 

Today, in our church, even those who have just entered the church are sent out alone to pioneer regions after receiving grace. 

Since you have received grace, go out to pioneer. If the leaves have grown lush, you must grow as one stalk. From now on, you must bear unique content with the value of the infinite fruition of heaven and earth centered around your own individuality. 

Many trials will come. Elements and essences that oppose your own vitality will flow in and out, rebelling against your life. You must possess the infinite subjective ability to digest that rebellion, so that even if the outside appears dead, you must have life within. If you have that ability, you will grow in that environment. 

As the connections of spring, summer, and autumn deepen, the leaves of the tree will reach their end. The color of that tree will change. Similarly, if you walk this path, others will see you and feel that you possess a mature fruition that no one can follow in that aspect. 

In this way, during the autumn season, there is no need to ask others to see your fruitful appearance. There is no need to sigh just because they do not recognize you. When you enter a time when you can complete all the contents of that value, all things will protect you and exist for you. Therefore, when the autumn season of value is revealed, it goes without saying that you can be preserved by God as a being of hope that can make a new start in the future. 

Advance until the end and become the master of all seasons
Such a time of grace exists for everyone. The time when you first entered the church can be called the spring season. The next is the time of walking alone. You must understand that there is a time to bear fruit alone by adding the essence of life. 

That is why in our church, complex matters such as being children of faith are developed. 

You must possess the vitality to overcome trials and pains in the environment that is approaching. Centered around a united self, you must become the embodiment of the total vitality of spring, summer, and autumn, and welcome the autumn season.
We must be unified to overcome. Whether it is A, B, or C, everyone must gather into one life force. With this, we must overcome and transcend the autumn season.

9) The Path of World Restoration  
<Summary of the Words> The history of restoration providence is the history of Abel overcoming Cain. To save Cain, Abel must make a sacrifice, and to make that sacrifice, he must bear the cross. By doing so, we must conquer the world of Satan through the work of saving Cain.  
Why do we send out local pioneering evangelism in our church? Going to the village is to find the Cain-like responsible person in the village, going to the district is to find the Cain-like responsible person in the district, and going to the province is to find the Cain-like responsible person in the province.  
What should we do when we find them? We must carry out a history of taking back by placing the condition of being a sacrifice. This requires sacrifice. In other words, blood must be shed, and that blood must be shed by Abel.  
Now, the Unification Church has reached the era where it can fulfill Abel's mission in a denominational way. Therefore, you should pay attention to the pastors and elders of established churches. And pay attention to the members of established churches. In showing interest, we should not regard them as enemies but should pay attention to the point where we can be recognized as being more for them than the established church pastors.  
Aren't Cain and Abel brothers who separated 6,000 years ago? Yet their reunion has extended through 6,000 years of personal struggles, familial struggles, and national struggles to our time. Now, the struggle has reached its peak, and it is time for reconciliation, a chance to meet again. Therefore, we must use Abel's strategy to overcome Cain, just as Jacob used a strategy to overcome Esau.  
That is why we are actively supporting Japan's Soka Gakkai to confront the Japanese Communist Party. They are all amazed and grateful. We opposed them, yet they are impressed that we are helping them when they were in a bind.  
So now, when you return to your local areas, make sure to show that we care for established church members more than their pastors care for them. Mobilize all our members to support established churches, and when they hold revival meetings, go and evangelize for them. During this special six-month period, understand and sympathize with the pastors who actively support established churches.  
When you pray, you must also pray for established churches.  
I recognize my brother, but he does not recognize me and treats me like an enemy. We must enlighten him to this fact, but how will we enlighten him? To do so, we must serve him with unspoken results. Then, in the end, won't my brother realize, apologize, and return? That is why we are told to love our enemies.  
Next, we must lead established churches and work for the nation. Thus, when the nation is restored, that is, when South Korea becomes united centered on God and fully armed with unification thought, the North Korean Communist Party will automatically surrender. Why? Because we already have the data that can make them collapse based on the results we have from fighting in Japan and other parts of Asia. When that happens, the path of world restoration will automatically open up.  
<Instructions>  
◆ Issues of Member Life  
No matter how difficult it is, do not rely on your family. Take the position of having a grievance for not being able to provide. Then God will command the family members to help.  
◆ Issues of Member Training  
We need to re-educate the members. We are short on members. Securing talent is a serious issue. Focus more on high school graduates and aim to evangelize three high school graduates each month to send to training sessions. The work of heaven starts from the small people. We should not disregard those who came from the bottom.  
Focus on one-on-one operations.  
◆ Establishing the 3.7 Scholarship Fund  
We should establish a scholarship fund in connection with the 700 couple joint wedding ceremony. Work hard in every way for that.  
◆ Others  
District leaders should continue to give Principle lectures, and when lecturing, they should do so while sweating. After giving victory lectures, please organize the structure. Actively utilize magazines such as "Modern and New Theological Christian Thought" published by Yonsei University.  
Again, for those who have attended victory lectures, please organize circles in the form of victory joint meetings according to each situation. Also, organize their support groups to maintain effectiveness.  
From May, primarily meet one-on-one and focus on personal evangelism. The target should be for nurturing key members. The main slogan from May to August will be one-on-one persuasive evangelism.

Conditions Necessary for the Fulfillment of Purpose

In living, there is always a purpose that must be achieved. Centered around that purpose, we must walk for 10 years, 20 years, 30 years… 70 years, a lifetime. The greater the purpose, the more resolutely we must commit ourselves internally. Without that, we cannot reach the purpose. Unless we continue to maintain an internal resolution that can surpass that purpose through the process of time, we cannot achieve that purpose.

In the process of an individual achieving a purpose, various connections and circumstances collide. In pushing forward for the fulfillment of a purpose, there may be environments that welcome us on our path, but there are far more conditions that oppose and hinder that purpose, appearing several times over. This is a fact we feel in our lives. Thus, when we cannot overcome the opposing environment and collapse under the pressure, we bring about the sorrowful results of frustration and failure.

We see this fact often in our lives, in society, and in the world. Thus, we experience that there are proportionally more conditions opposing us than those welcoming us on our path.

If there is a great person who is trying to run toward a great purpose, the greater that purpose is, the more it encompasses nations and the world. The events that arise are not conditions of welcome on the path of that great person but rather conditions of conflict and opposition. The greater the opposing factors that appear, the greater the factors of despair and failure can also be.

Therefore, when such events arise, the person responsible for those events must appear as a core entity of greater resolution and concentrated strength than the events themselves. Without confronting difficult environments, one cannot resolve those events. Thus, the position of a person who must resolve such environments cannot be taken lightly. To overcome such issues, one must have a stronger conviction regarding the purpose. How to express the internal impulse that can surpass the external trials is the key to solving that problem.

Humans have tried to overcome such problems every time they encounter them in their life journey, but they have repeatedly failed. This has been the norm of human life. So what does God, who knows this, require of us? He desires us to make repeated resolutions and commitments. We will inevitably face trials ahead, so we must resolve ourselves again to prepare for those trials. To achieve a great purpose by overcoming external environments, we must introduce a strength and stimulus that is stronger than the approaching trials. This is the most important issue. This is not only a matter of concern for God but also an important issue that we ourselves must resolve.

When faced with such a position, people need a stronger force. Because they need a more stimulating factor, they seek a third force. The greater the person, the more they understand that they cannot reinforce the strength to overcome the trials in ordinary social environments. Thus, it is inevitable that great people will need a third force.

However, since this cannot come from humans, they seek a power stronger than themselves and stimuli beyond what they currently feel, and at such times, they turn to God. We see this fact often through biographies of great figures.

To overcome trials

You must prepare with sincerity for such environments, such lives, and such moments. Knowing that the conditions of the approaching trials are great, you must pour out all your intelligence. When you do not know what kind of trials will come in the future or when they will come, you must always live cautiously and with sincerity in a position where you can unite with God. You must continue such a life to reinforce the strength to overcome the upcoming trials.

From this perspective, the purpose of a person living a life of faith is not merely to achieve personal victory, but the world is the purpose, so the path of a believer heading toward that great purpose cannot be a path of easy suffering. Therefore, the path each of you must take is not a smooth one.

This path is one that must be walked with desperation as you feel the environment that can lead to the failure of countless human resolutions. This path is one of difficult trials and cannot be a path of misery.

So what is the one secret to overcoming those trials? It is sufficient for the internal resolution to be greater than the approaching trials. In other words, one must stand in a subjective position that can create the strength to cope with external trials. However, if one is in a position where they cannot reinforce such strength while walking the path of faith, they must always maintain an attitude aligned with God.

The path of trials I am walking is not just my path; it is also the path that God must walk. However, since God cannot walk without humans, He must establish a person to walk, or He must walk through someone else if not through me. Thus, I must stand in a position where I represent many people, pouring out my sincerity and saying that God's will is my will, and only then can I establish a connection with God, and through that, I can receive a new strength that has not existed in my environment until now. This is the life of a believer.

The greater the person responsible for history and the global mission, the more they need the resolution to overcome the trials and tribulations of the times, rather than just the internal resolution to overcome the trials they aim for. If that trial is global, a resolution to overcome it at a global level is necessary. To sustain that resolution, one must establish an internal relationship with God that no one else knows about. This is a given fact.

Therefore, when there are difficult problems, we should desire to discuss them with God rather than with humans. And we must feel that it is far more valuable to share our circumstances and discuss them with God than with any individual. We can understand from history that without such experiences, we cannot bear difficult missions.

In this regard, those of you standing on the path of our Unification Church today have personal paths of indemnity ahead of you. The personal indemnity path must come to an end at some point before a foundation can be established to relate to God. Then, based on that foundation, one can take on public responsibilities. In other words, one cannot be responsible for the public indemnity path without going through a process that can indemnify oneself. To be responsible for the public indemnity path, one must go through their own indemnity path.

When we analyze our own indemnity paths, they all bear historical significance, as they are inherited from our ancestors. Here, if many of our ancestors are good ancestors, that may be fine, but the less good the ancestors are, the greater the conditions of indemnity attached to oneself will be proportionally.

To resolve the conditions of indemnity

When we come to know such facts, the issue becomes how to surpass the limits of our own indemnity before embarking on the public indemnity path. So, when thinking about the individual indemnity path, how much indemnity must one's individual self surpass? Some may have to surpass ten, some a hundred, some a thousand, and some may have to surpass ten thousand.

When we look at the myriad human forms today, the indemnity shapes imposed on each person behind them can also be said to be myriad. Anyone who uses someone as a standard to say, "He is a happy person," is foolish. The happiness they refer to is not connected to the individual. It is historical. That is, it appears through the good deeds of their ancestors.
The virtuous ancestors lived a public life while failing to achieve a happy life. Among his ancestors, many passed through the journey of life centered on their personal happiness, rather than standing in a public position and leading an unhappy life. They left behind their public contributions while walking such an unfortunate path. For them, there remains a foundation of public service where they consumed their reality and life for the hope of the future.

Those who were built upon the foundation of such ancestors, in other words, descendants born on the foundation where their ancestors have already paid the price of future sacrifices, will live happier than anyone in society until the period of remission arrives at a certain limit in the future. In other words, they will live within a realm of blessed living.

The more one is born from the standpoint of their ancestors who have paid the price of remission, the happier they must be at the present moment. However, when such people see countless others who still have the content of remission remaining, they may wish, "How wonderful it would be if I could live happily like them!" but they cannot live that way. No matter how much they wish for it, it cannot happen. The more they desire it, the more compounded trials and the compounded contents of remission will come before them. We must understand that the more we hope for that happiness to be realized in a short period, the more the compounded factors of remission will confront us.

Therefore, we must know how much remission we need to settle before stepping into a public position. If someone can guess how much remission remains, when it comes to settling it in a year or a month, there probably won't be anyone who wants to settle it over a year. Everyone would want to settle it all in a month. However, if one tries to settle it in a month, they will face trials multiplied tenfold, and the question becomes whether they are prepared to endure such trials.

To settle such remission conditions in a month, one cannot remain in the same position. There must be a vow, and there are certainly conditions for making such a vow. Even worldly people make vows by swearing on a knife or by putting something else at stake. Similarly, in order to shorten the period of remission that lies ahead, one must make an internal vow and resolution that corresponds to it, and there must be conditions that can counterbalance the remission conditions.

A sacrifice is presented as a condition in making a new promise between God and oneself. Therefore, when offering such sacrifices, one must be clear about what they are for. Just as there is no vow without a purpose, there is also no sacrifice without a purpose.

To walk the path of remission, time must be consumed. Moreover, it is not just the consumption of time; there must also be a consumption of oneself. Therefore, what is presented as a condition to prevent the consumption of oneself is the sacrifice. You must understand this.

Private Remission Path and Public Remission Path
Each of you has the responsibility to pioneer this path of faith. Then, how much time have you consumed here, and how much of yourself have you spent? This will determine whether you can remove the factors of remission or not.

When thinking about this, what kind of path is the path of faith today? As you know, it is a path of sacrifice. So what kind of sacrifice is this? It is the sacrifice of one's life. In other words, it is the path of investing all factors that can make oneself happy. Furthermore, one's physical body must also be involved in this. In other words, one must pay the price of sacrifice centered on the whole and the price of sacrifice centered on oneself. The longer the time and the greater the amount of personal sacrifice, the more proportionately one can settle the amount of remission for their lifetime.

If you are living a life of faith to settle remission, you must clearly distinguish whether that remission is private or public. Today, there is clearly such a path of remission before the members of our Unification Church. Ordinary people do not know their path of remission. They are unaware of the journey of remission they must undertake. However, God cannot help but guide such people, even if vaguely, toward a path of remission.

That is why when God commands us, He does not say, "Sacrifice for yourself." He says to sacrifice for others or for the family. What does it mean to sacrifice for the family? It means to settle the conditions of remission not from a personal standpoint but from a higher position. In other words, He encourages us not to settle for today’s path but to settle for the future that lies ahead.

Those who have paid the price of remission for the coming era can move forward. Those who settle for today cannot remain for tomorrow, but those who settle for the future can remain for today. What this means is that those who take responsibility for the place of settling for the future can surpass today’s process of remission.

Therefore, when considering the flow of history, what is the mainstream thought? It is sacrifice. Today, human morality emphasizes sacrifice. Sacrificial service centered on the family and sacrificial service for the nation is the universal path for any individual or nation. Thus, in the family, we are told to honor our parents and serve the nation. This means to extend the content of remission that one bears until the future.

Loyalty for the future is loyalty for the multitude. The sincerity I put forth is not just for myself. Although one person may put forth their sincerity, the influence of that sincerity reaches the entire nation. Therefore, if the population of that nation is ten thousand, all ten thousand must respond to me.

Among those ten thousand, there will be many who are greater than I. Those great people, from a relative standpoint, will bless me, look up to me, and encourage me to be blessed, creating a natural environment that can connect the conditions of Cain and Abel to a grand stage.

Thus, my personal sincerity does not end with myself but extends to those living in the environment related to me. Among that multitude, there may be descendants of virtuous ancestors who have walked the path of remission I am currently walking. When such people bow their heads and praise me, it is something that God cannot help but remember.

A person who has ten, a hundred, or a thousand people remembering them cannot help but be remembered by God. If they pray for me and bless me for the efforts I made to bless them, then the conditions of my personal remission will be automatically settled due to their prayers and for their sake.

The Expectation of Sincerity Where God Can Be Present
God has established such an environment in the historical process and has led countless humans not to bring them suffering but to grant each individual the authority to receive blessings more than anyone else within that era. This operation is to make one sacrifice from a public position.

Therefore, the more people there are who pray and sincerely care for me, the more blessed that person must be. To have many people sincerely caring for one person, one must first give all the blessings they have to many people. Before that, one must understand that many people will not bless me.

If ten people sincerely care for one person, that person cannot help but be remembered by God. Let us expand the environment where we can stimulate each other to a new stage by managing the environment in which we sincerely care for one another. The organization that has been formed to achieve this is the church. Therefore, the leaders of the church must not be sincere for themselves but must be sincere for the multitude.

The multitude they must care for is not only their own family but also the nation and the world. That is why the perspective of church leaders must not be limited to their own family and church members. They must have a heart that can reach the nation and the world through their church members, praying, "Please pave the way for us to go out into the world with the sincerity I have offered and the sincerity of the church members."

When the church leaders and members unite in this way, God will surely be present among them. When God is present in unity, it is not for the revival of the church but for the revival of the nation. Therefore, that church will not perish until the nation becomes one. Furthermore, if there is a church that sincerely works for the unity of the world, that church will not perish until the world becomes one.

What enabled Christianity to pioneer world history today? Even as Jesus Christ faced the fate of dying on the cross, He said, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will." Here, what is the boundary of the Father’s will? It is the world. That is why He transcended the frontiers for the world and endured all the suffering of shedding blood.

Faithful followers who follow that central Christ must embody the heart of Christ, saying, "I will go for the purpose of Christ who died for the world." Just as Christ walked the path of death, I will also walk that path, fulfilling my duty of loyalty before God. Those who resolve to shed the blood and sweat of loyal subjects and filial children will bring about a revolutionary and progressive history for the world. To do so, an infinite price of sacrifice must be paid.

However, where is the limit of that sacrifice? If one has appealed for the development of their church, then that church will reach a limit, meaning it will end at the end of the century. However, a church that has become a historical altar of martyrdom for humanity and the world will govern history and will not perish even after settling the end.

From this perspective, when we observe the sincere efforts of Christianity today, there may be many groups praying for a day when the global Christian community can triumph, but how many Christians have sincerely cared and walked the path of death to save even the enemies who will be judged at the end? The number is not large. This is something we can understand by observing the current phenomenon of the end of Christianity.

What should our Unification Church be today? We do not need Unification Church members for the sake of the Unification Church. Our Unification Church must stand in a position that serves the nation, and it will remain until the nation develops. When we sincerely work for the world, it will remain until the world remains. If we invest our sincerity toward something beyond the world, we will digest the world and remain in a place beyond that.

From this perspective, the Unification Church advocates for a universalism that transcends the world. This is not a vague statement. This content is closely related to the life of remission we are living today. Then, how many people feel this fact? The more one feels it vividly, the more that person will be a great individual. Why is that person great? Because they stand in a position to face the trials that will come before the world and the universe and vow to struggle against them. Even if the time they desire may be a thousand or two thousand years later, and they may become a martyr today and a sacrifice, they will, regardless, pave the point of victory in the historical era before God, who transcends time.

From this perspective, today, the members of our Unification Church must think. So, who is a wise person? A person who walks the path of suffering only for personal remission is a foolish person. After all, the path of personal remission must be walked. It must be settled. However, there may be people who cannot settle their remission through their lifetime due to the great amount of remission inherited from their ancestors. If such people sincerely care for their personal remission, that sincerity will have no impact on the future.

However, if they go beyond their personal interests and resolve to be a sacrifice, saying, "I am the sacrifice. My life itself is the sacrifice. My life itself is the condition of a vow that represents history," then even if that itself is insufficient, it allows them to establish a condition of a vow with God centered on the future world, transcending the limits of history.

Where one is prepared to face death, there is nothing they cannot vow. We must become people who are willing to risk our lives. When we risk our lives and make an appeal centered on the world, it becomes an appeal to the world.

Therefore, we must become those who vow before God, saying, "I will dedicate my life as a sacrifice for humanity, for the world, and for the universe." 

Thus, a person who vows to fully invest their life for a purpose and appears as a sacrifice can automatically settle not only the factors of remission for their lifetime but also the factors of remission for their ancestors and clan. 

History has been purified by their blood price and their martyrdom, and it has continued to this present era. When considering this fact, there must be a path of remission before the members of our Unification Church today. There is the personal path of remission. Only after going through that personal path of remission can one walk the public path of remission. This is a just perspective centered on the holy place called heaven.

As fallen descendants, we humans find it extremely difficult to stand in a holy place before the holy God. That is why it is not cruel for God, who is advancing the providential will, to push His beloved sons and daughters toward the path of death. It is because that is a secret method to bless them that He cannot help but lead them down that path. We must understand this aspect of God.

There will be times when trials come even when we are walking without any thoughts. At such times, we should not try to avoid those trials. Even if one has not made a vow, when the leader of their organization has made a vow, they may fall into the conditions of trials presented by that leader and be caught up in remission. What does this mean? It means that if the leader of that organization fails, they may also encounter the fate of failure.

Then, why do I, who did not even think about it, receive the influence of remission when the one who set the conditions for remission is the leader? It is because if the sovereign of a nation sets the conditions for remission and remits, the people of that nation also share in the remission with the sovereign.
The path corresponding to that indemnity is like having to walk the road of suffering. Today, Korea is in the process of development centered around the five-year economic development plan, and the people are participating and following as planned by the government. When the government faces difficulties, the people must also inevitably face hardships. The achievement of that purpose is not separate from one another. The people are influenced by the government within their living sphere. Our indemnity law is the same.

Moreover, the sovereigns of that nation will be directly affected. If the world enters the era of indemnity, then all of humanity will be influenced by the global era of indemnity. You must understand that this is how indemnity is transcended. 

So, what kind of person is a wise person? A wise person is one who inherits the victorious connection of the historical era. In other words, it is someone who inherits something of greater value. To inherit something of greater value, one must go through a greater process of indemnity in life. Therefore, the path of indemnity is a fateful path that we must walk. 

All members living centered around the Unification Church today must go through a historical process that can resolve the indemnity conditions presented by the teacher. If you do not go in the direction indicated by God from an external standpoint, you must receive indemnity internally. When you align your steps toward the direction your will is aiming for, an internal battle will inevitably occur. An external battle will arise simultaneously with an internal battle.

When the internal is consumed, it must be accompanied by external consumption to establish a connection. Without that, you cannot transcend the path of indemnity. Therefore, a wise person is someone who acts for that purpose. 

That is why today, the Unification Church cannot help but demand action from you. Forcing action is a miserable thing. However, if it does not end in misery but rather is overcome, it becomes a condition to not only walk the path of indemnity for today but also to walk the path of the offerings sworn before the public path of indemnity for tomorrow. When this period exceeds three years, it can remain there.

It is essential that from the four realms, God's intervention occurs. We understand this from the principle.

It must be a sincerity that can impact world history. There will be unspeakable trials there. The world you are looking at will come crashing down before your eyes. At that moment, you must seize that moment and ride the great wave that comes, pushing everything forward instead. This is the first chance that has appeared in 6,000 years of history. The fact that God emphasizes this chance and grants it to us is due to His great love. Therefore, those who lose this period of being able to receive love are exceedingly foolish. 

Centered around this content, Jesus also walked a period of three years. Because he could not fulfill his purpose in that three-year period, he decided to establish at least a three-day period, risking his life to pray earnestly for three days. This is the path that Jesus Christ walked, and you must understand this. 

Jesus Christ lost the public three-year path of indemnity in world history, so he struggled with the question of how to connect the private three-day period with the global connection, praying, "Not my will, but Yours be done," and also praying to forgive his enemies, after which he declared that it was all accomplished. What does this mean? It means that not only was the indemnity of Jesus' lifetime fulfilled, but his desire to connect it with the historical indemnity connection was also realized. 

Now, will you invest your life for private indemnity, or will you invest your life for public indemnity? It is the same to invest your life, but what is the difference? Those who risk their lives to invest their life in the public environment for public indemnity cannot be anything but great figures. A new history will be established because of such people. 

Then, how will we fill the remaining time before such moments? This is now the trial path you must walk. Therefore, whether you live your life personally or publicly becomes an issue. In your own life, everything you eat, wear, buy, and sell is for whom? Is it for yourself or for God? Another issue is whether that is a public life or a private life. Also, whether your emotions are private emotions or public emotions is also a problem. 

To walk the public path, shouldn't you seek a place to make a vow? Anyone who bears the mission to indemnify history must advance to the place they desire. Thus, in life, transcending private emotions and how to acquire public emotions is a matter that a believer must prioritize. 

What is sin? Sin arises from private places. Destruction also occurs from private standards. Evil is the same. When the private exceeds its limit, it manifests as evil. There is a limit to the private, and when that limit is exceeded, it becomes evil, leads to destruction, and commits sin. 

Then, where is the place that can be eternally good, prosper, and be blessed? Where is the place that can avoid destruction, sin, and evil? That place is precisely the public place. Even when eating, it must be in a public place. Even when working, it must be public work, and even when speaking, it must be public words. In this way, everything must be lived in connection with the public. Such a person cannot go to hell. 

The secret to going to heaven is this: how public are you? Who is the close person who can pave the way for you to stand on the public stage? That is your brothers. The path of restoration is the path of pioneering the public way, so the way for the sons and daughters standing in the public position is only the way of serving their brothers. To walk the public path, there is no other way but to care for one another. 

Therefore, the person in the Abel position must be a model in caring for their brothers. By doing so, they must lead those in the Cain position to follow them and become one with them. Then, because all brothers stand in the public position, they become good and prosper. Everything is like this. 

The more public existence is Abel. Among the members of the Unification Church, some think they are Abel because they came in first, but if they cannot stand in the public position even if they came in first, they are Cain. Without a doubt, they are Cain. Even though Cain was born first, he had to follow Abel because he was not in a public position. 

Among the Unification Church members, there may be someone who stubbornly claims, "I came in first, so I am Abel." However, if they cannot stand in a public position compared to someone who came in later, what are they? "They are Cain." They are Cain. The one called Abel is a thief. The Abel-like existence is the one who stands in a more public position. 

Then, what kind of relationship should you have to walk the public path? You must have a brotherly relationship. In seeking cooperation to walk the public path, saying, "Father, let’s do this" will not work. However, saying, "Brother, let’s do this" or "Younger brother, let’s do this" is acceptable. The horizontal relationship is important in walking the public path. 

In going to heaven, it is not a matter of becoming one with God. The secret to going to heaven is to walk the public path. 

In walking this public path, brothers are necessary. Without holding hands with your brothers, you cannot expand the more public environment, so even if your older or younger brother is a sinner, you must forgive them. This public path must be walked absolutely, so even if there are only sinners and enemies before you, you must forgive and love them. Otherwise, you cannot walk the public path. Love is an essential requirement for walking the public path. 

You must know these principles and live according to them. If you know the principles and live according to your own way, you will fail. Even if the principles remain, you yourself will not remain. You must live a principled life with the mindset that you want to remain alongside the principles. Your heart and body must move in unity with the principles. Thus, what moves in that way must remain as public before humanity and in the historical era. 

Do you wish to become that way? If so, stand in a public position. If you wish for things to go well from a private standpoint, you will fail. If you focus on your desires in your neighborhood, you will be struck in that neighborhood. Isn’t that so? Even if you are told not to hate, you will hate. 

You may think, "When will that guy fall? When will that old lady collapse?" This is how it becomes. If everyone in the neighborhood thinks like that, that person will be punished. 

The path of sacrificing for others is the path of receiving blessings. Until now, religion has taught this, and ethics and morality have also taught this. In light of this, you must understand that it is not God who judges to destroy history and humanity, but God who comes to grant blessings to humanity. 

God, who knows that the path of principles cannot be walked without loving your enemies, will He destroy all of humanity through judgment at the end? No. God is in the position of a parent toward humanity. The so-called non-judgment spoken of in Christianity today is not non-judgment in the literal sense. 

Love your children from a public standpoint
Today, the world must walk hand in hand with various nations. If it is the Republic of Korea, then with the Republic of Korea; if it is Japan, then with Japan, and so on with other Asian countries. When it is time to emphasize this the most, it means that the public era of world history has come before our eyes. 

When viewed from the perspective of this principle, the story of a nation does not end with the trials of that nation but becomes a global trial. When the day comes when the world is swirling, it can be seen that a public nation of peace will emerge. At that time, the question will be whether humanity can unite or not, and if all the citizens of every country do not live only for their own country but resolve to live for the world and only care for one another, the world will prosper. 

When water swirls and creates a whirlpool, a guide is needed. Therefore, when the world is swirling and creating a whirlpool, you must find a path. In the midst of that, you must present a way forward. Thus, we say to unite and become one. That is why we advocate for the principle of Heavenism. We are saying to follow the public laws of Heaven. You must clearly understand that this is the assertion of the Unification Church. You may seem to be going along without any thought, but in reality, you are walking the path of indemnity. Therefore, after understanding the will, if you do nothing, you may think it will be comfortable, but it will not be. 

When you see the teacher, don’t you feel sorry? In the past, you lived as you pleased and had nothing to envy in the world, but now that you know the will, you realize it is not so. Therefore, when the teacher gives any instructions, you should be grateful. Then your heart will be indemnified. 

You know that historically, Korean people have always presented their hands neatly when approaching elders. That has been the custom. When you follow the principles, you will find comfort. Do you understand what I mean? 

Do you wish to be blessed? Do you wish for eternal life? To do so, you must become a public person. In educating your children, do not love them only as your own sons and daughters. You must become parents who love them as sacrificial sons and daughters for the world. And when you hold your children in your arms and breastfeed them, you must do so with the mindset of a mother representing humanity on this planet, feeding the child who represents humanity. And do not only feed your own children with affection, but become a mother who treats others' children as if they were your own. The babies raised on such a mother’s milk will surely become great people. Even if it does not happen immediately, through one or two generations, they will grow into greatness.
A figure capable of ruling the world will be born among those descendants. This is a certainty. It will happen.

After offering sincerity before God and pledging for tomorrow, the steps taken are always restored with a strong force of stimulation. <Words> As you all know, today is the last day of May. May comes to an end today, and from tomorrow we will welcome June. The spring season has passed, and the summer season is upon us. When we look at an event, there are motives, processes, and results leading up to that event. And whether the result is good or bad is determined by how it manifests. The achievement of the goal set at the beginning is determined by the results that appear. 

If a person who aimed for a result of 100 achieved more than 100, then all the days spent to achieve that result, all the time that flowed from the motive to the process, gains absolute value, and that person can claim it. However, if the goal was 100 and it does not reach 100 or results in failure, then all the time from the motive to the process becomes a time of resentment, sorrow, and a time one would rather not recall. Similarly, when we look at the flowing historical era centered on the purpose, the most important question is how the results left by history are determined in relation to that purpose. 

If the purpose is great, there will be a proportional consumption of time. And to fulfill the purpose, human effort must be invested along with time.

The issue is whether the time and human effort invested during that period became sorrow or joy.
