Besides the day Adam and Eve were born, the day they held their wedding ceremony or the day they came to this earth and returned would have been celebrated by all of humanity as long as human history continued through the ages. Nevertheless, considering the fact that no one has thought about such days until now, we must recognize that this is an unspeakably sad matter. 
If a global unity had been formed to commemorate the day Adam was born, the day he was married, and the day he returned, humanity celebrating such days would have become one brotherhood and one people. In other words, they could have become humans living in one world. If that had happened, all the customs that Adam lived by would have been inherited in human history, and the culture formed at that time would have been passed down forever. 
However, when we look at this world today, we see that the Republic of Korea has a specific cultural background. Countless nations have different histories and traditions. This is a tragic fact. Originally, if a tribe had been formed that reproduced from one set of parents, centered around one purpose, able to communicate with each other, respecting the ties of one child and the ties of one parent, the culture of that tribe would have been inherited from the roots established in the time of Adam. 
All the customs of life that Adam lived by, such as language and etiquette, should have been inherited as they were, and the languages and cultures of this world should have been unified; however, they have appeared in various forms. The reason for this diversity is that conflicts arose. In other words, a slaughtering war broke out between Cain and Abel in Adam's family. Thus, from that time onward, division began, and you must understand this. 
Humanity, inheriting this historical tradition, has fought fiercely through the ages, even among the same brothers, and after a major fight, they have separated based on the principle that what he likes, I must dislike unconditionally. Thus, the culture of humanity has been formed in various branches. When the elder brother says "rice," the younger brother does not call it rice. Every time he encounters rice, he recalls the bad memories with his elder brother, so he expressed rice in his own way. Consequently, their lives also differed. Ultimately, it is through this hostility that culture has been divided. 
The fundamental reason why all humanity could not become one nation and was divided into various nations lies here. Of course, there is a biblical saying that this happened while building the Tower of Babel, but we cannot overlook the fact that division occurred because each person prioritized their own purpose. Therefore, humanity could not possess the original cultural sphere and original living sphere that all humanity could leave behind and share. This is a retribution due to the fall.

The meaning of tithing and the management of all things 
When looking at the Christian practice of tithing, one can see that it contains truly profound content. There are biblical verses that state one must give a tithe. It says to dedicate one out of ten to God. 

However, does God appear? There may be those who ask what tithing is, but what tithing signifies is that by giving one, one is committing to the whole. If you were to prepare a feast for your parents' birthday or a celebration for a significant milestone, would they consume everything you offer? No. They would accept it all but would not be able to eat it all, consuming only a small portion. However, even though they only eat a little, the condition is established that they have received everything. 

In the same way, tithing means dedicating one-tenth of the material one possesses to God, symbolizing the offering of the whole. While one does not offer the entire amount to the Father, dedicating one with sincerity holds value in that sense. By offering that one, the remaining nine are treated as holy. A person who lives by tithing will never experience failure. As time goes on, their storehouses will continue to grow.

Water must also be kept clean. Thus, all things are public. 

The sun is the source of life and has infinite value. We receive that sunlight for free. Have you ever seen someone carrying money to buy sunlight? Have you ever seen anyone who has paid even a penny for sunlight? If sunlight were to be sold, would you buy it or not? You would buy it even if it meant giving up your body. All natural resources like water, air, and light are not yours. Anyone who thinks of these things as their own is a thief. 

Who is the owner of all things? Before it is mine, it belongs to the nation, and before it belongs to the nation, it belongs to the world. Why is that? Let’s consider this. Before our nation's founding father, Dangun, appeared, whose land was this? Was there an owner? Is there an owner according to public law? When looking only at people, there is no owner, but in terms of public law, there is an owner. So who is the owner? God is the owner. Is that owner the owner of the world or the owner of the Republic of Korea? That owner is the owner of the world before being the owner of the Republic of Korea. So who is the owner of this world? Is the owner of the world the United States? Because God existed before America, God is the owner of this world. 

Then who should govern this land? Naturally, it should be God, the owner of the world, who governs. Otherwise, the person who is most loved by God, who represents the owner, should govern. If there is a son who receives the most love from God and is asked whose country America is, he can claim it as his own. If asked whose world it is, he can also say it is his own. A person who receives more love from God than others can confidently claim that this world is theirs. 

That is why you should not boast about being a patriot of the United States. You must know that the owner of the United States is God. Therefore, the person who has a worldview that is loyal to God governs the world. If you prioritize American ideology and make that the national ideology, America will perish. To ensure humanity's eternal existence, we must adopt God as the owner and strive to create one world, in other words, a more valuable world, a more eternal world. What is that ideology? It is the ideology of God. If you become a son or daughter who receives God's love, you can say that the world is yours. 

If someone buys the best house in the Republic of Korea, and their little son comes and says, "Dad, our house is really nice!" is there a father who would respond, "Why is it our house? It is mine"? "We" means half belongs to the father and half belongs to the son, but is there a parent who would feel bad hearing such a thing? No. Every parent would say, "Yes, it is our house. You know well." 

Why is that? Because love creates oneness. The bond between parents and children is established through love. Therefore, there is no father who can break that love, and there is no child who can break that love. Only love governs both, so the things connected through love are undoubtedly the property of both the parent and the child. In this sense, God loved the world so much that He gave His only begotten Son, so that whoever believes in Him shall not perish but have eternal life (John 3:16). God did not send His only begotten Son to be persecuted and die on the cross. He sent Him to be loved. 

If there is a precious item placed in the church, and if others do not value that item, is it public behavior or private behavior for you to take it home? "It is private behavior." That is private behavior. If it is private behavior, then it is theft, right? It is placed there because it has value. Even if you might think it has no value and treat it as such, it does not mean it has no value. 

For example, in a palace, the king, queen, and prince live there, but does the prince call the king or queen "Your Majesty" or "Your Highness"? They call them father, mother, son, daughter, brother, sister. The same applies here. However, can a prince take the property of the people as he pleases? He cannot. Just because he is a prince, can he take what the people do not take? 

He might think, "This might be useless here. If I take it, I will love it more and value it more, so I can't leave it here." Can he take it like that? No, he cannot. The environment is different, and there is a separate place where it should be. 

Today, Unification Church members must understand this. There have been times when valuable items in our Unification Church have disappeared. That is a sin. Everything has its rightful place. It may be acceptable at headquarters, but it should not happen in local areas. From this perspective, how you manage public property becomes an issue. 

Approach all things with a new heart and recognize their value. We must approach all things from this perspective. When looking at the rising sun, you should think, "Oh sun, you are shining so brightly, providing me with life, and I cannot buy you even with a fortune. You rise so beautifully to sustain my life." You should think, "Wow! How strong and admirable you are!" When looking at water, even if it flows pitifully, even the greatest man will swallow his pride and lick the dirt if he is thirsty. You should praise it as an amazing stream of water! Additionally, when you see a lone pine tree among many trees, instead of saying, "Why are you alone among so many trees?", you should say, "Oh, you are the only seed left after all the others have died." If you think like this, your perspective will change. 

Even when walking, if you carry such a heart and think in such a way, you cannot help but love your country and the world. When you say you truly love, what is the essence of that true love? It is God. Does God love the Republic of Korea more or the world more? He loves the world more. Then, does God love the world more or heaven and earth more? He loves heaven and earth more. He loves the greater things. The greater things are more public, which is why He loves the greater things. 

God loves the nation, loves the world, and loves the heavens and the earth, and He loves a nation that lives with the intention and ideology of loving them. Therefore, do not be discouraged just because you are currently poor, chased, and oppressed. Do you understand? Even if you have to eat corn rice or barley rice and dip it in salt or soybean paste, even if you see that soybean paste...
the holy soybean paste jar. If we say that, then that soybean paste jar becomes the world's best soybean paste jar. 

Even if it is a plate stained black and with missing teeth, the subject that treats you is another person. That’s what you should do. Then its value changes. The food on that plate may be insignificant, but at this moment, it will enter my body as holy food and give me strength. This strength will be used for the nation and for the world. Would that plate feel bad? How joyful would it be? You should sense the joy of that object as you enter a mysterious realm. You must reach such a state. 

That is why, if there is someone who loves an object more than themselves, that is, someone who has loved more publicly, they should give it to that person. If there is someone who loves you more than you love yourself, should you give them the ring or jewel you have, or not? When the ladies of the Unification Church pray, there are times when they are commanded in the spirit world to bring all the gold and valuables they possess to the teacher. What kind of God is this? Isn’t it the act of Reverend Moon using magic to take them away? 

You might think that, but that’s not it. What it means is that God recognizes something of greater value. And it means that the teacher is a little better than everyone else. 

If such an object can be used for the nation, it should not be used for one’s own children but sent to the nation. If it can be used for the world, it should be sent to the world. This is justice. This is the correct way to manage objects. Therefore, a person who loves their country and their people dedicates everything for the nation. They dedicate their possessions and even their families. 

The Difficulty of Public Life
The teacher does not teach you to live for Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. The teacher teaches you to live together with him for the nation and for the world. Incorrect teachings lead to destruction, and everyone packs their bags and leaves. If those teachings were not incorrect, even if they packed their bags and left, they would have to come back. Aren’t those who actually left now returning? 

Until now, the teacher has walked this path for over half a century, being chased and persecuted, but when he says to those who persecuted him, “If you compensate for the persecution you inflicted a thousandfold, you can be liberated,” there will come a time when both you and I will want to do such things without being forced to. If the public value has become more evident through suffering, then that environment also becomes valuable. When that happens, the environment will naturally be absorbed before the center. 

When we sell objects and earn money, we have to give a tithe, but how difficult is it to do this? It’s hard, isn’t it? Is there anything easy in public work? “No.” There is nothing easy. Also, we are told to wake up early and pray at dawn. Honestly, it is hard for the teacher too to pray after being woken up from sleep. (Laughter) It is not easy to wake up at around 4 a.m. to pray. Today is the Day of All Things, so I woke up around 1 a.m. There is a face to maintain in the spirit world, so I cannot help but pray. 

With sleepy eyes blinking, “Oh dear, today is the Day of All Things, so I must pray.” This is how difficult it is. Praying in the middle of the night when everyone else is asleep is a tough game. However, it must be done. Even if it is hard, it must be done to be comfortable. If I don’t pray, it feels very awkward to talk to you like this. 

If the teacher is even a little late for morning worship, he cannot hold his head up for the entire day. The teacher lives like this. If he looks at the clock and is even one minute late, his mood is ruined. For that whole day, and for that whole week, his mind is unsettled. Then the next week, he wakes up early and puts in tenfold or a hundredfold effort to make up for the mistakes of the previous week. By setting such conditions, his mind becomes at ease. This is how I live. So how pitiful is that? 

When the teacher talks to you, the type or appearance may seem nice, but because of that, he lives in a situation where he is bound for weeks or even months. Is this a private life or a public life? It is a public life. How nice it would be to live freely! If the teacher lived freely, he would live even more splendidly than you. I wouldn’t lose to anyone even if I danced. (Laughter) I have all kinds of talents. Even if I were to deceive others, I wouldn’t do anything trivial. If I did, I would at least rob the pockets of those who are recognized in Korea and say that I would return it only if they submit to me. 

In fact, you do not know how difficult the position of a religious leader is. He has to watch the eyes of everyone in the neighborhood and also the eyes of the utterly useless sinners. Of course, he must also watch the eyes of the capable people. He lives in a world where he has to be careful of everyone’s gaze. So, whether it’s a hit or a miss, it’s a big deal, and in this era of great powers, it’s even more so. There is no day or night. Doesn’t God see at night? Day and night, it’s a game of survival. This is the kind of game I am living. After living, it becomes a number. However, that number is a pitiful number. It can only be that of a manager. 

From that perspective, if you have lived like that, through whom does God work? He works through such people. God goes back and forth to a nation that is heading towards a more public world. What does this mean? If there is a nation that walks a more public path, God carries his bundle and goes to that nation. If there is an even more public nation, he adjusts his direction towards that one. This is how God goes back and forth. 

You must know how to manage publicly
You should not boast that you joined the Unification Church before others. According to the principle of Cain and Abel, Abel must be better than Cain. Abel must stand in a more public position than Cain. Just because you joined first and have dedicated everything from your youthful days until now, over 60 years old, you should not complain that you are not recognized. 

You must know the public management laws regarding all things. You must also know the public management laws regarding love. When one knows the public management laws better than their parents, they can take their children away. Do you understand? Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is doing such things now. He has taken the sons and daughters of others and married them as he pleases. When he blessed the 36 families, their parents came and complained, “Where in the world is there such a law? Who sent out the invitations for our sons and daughters?” So, the teacher boldly said that he did. It was because he stood in a more public position than their parents. 

At that time, I thought, “You don’t know now, but just wait a little while. Then you will know whether the son-in-law or daughter-in-law you received is better or not.” Not long after, the parents of those blessed families acknowledged that although they had done everything wrong, they had indeed received good sons-in-law and daughters-in-law. There was no way to excuse that. 

That is why how to manage public materials, how to manage individuals, how to manage families, how to manage society, how to manage the nation, and furthermore, how to manage the world must be established based on these public management laws. This principle is not humanism. It is not the principle of Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. If it were such a principle, it would lead to destruction. Whether one becomes one with God’s principle or not is what determines life and death. 

You must understand that standing in a more public position is more valuable, more eternal, and carries more weight. If a nation stands in a more public position than anything else, that nation will receive the heavenly fortune that can receive God’s blessings. You must clearly understand that heavenly fortune has come to the Republic of Korea. 

When eating with friends, some friends think, “I should pay this time since I’ve already had lunch three times,” but they just look around. Other friends gauge whether to pay or not by looking at that friend’s face. They hold out until the last spoon is placed down, and when one friend pays, they think, “I’m glad I didn’t pay.” That person is truly foolish. At that moment, they were happy holding onto the money with their fingers, but what are those fingers? They are preparing to stamp the mark of death. Their descendants will surely become the children of servants in a few generations. This is an undeniable fact. 

However, if one spends money for personal use while hesitating and saving, but spends that money for the nation, that person will never fail. There is a saying in the world, right? “Earn money freely and spend it well.” For something great, it’s okay to deceive one person to earn money. If one sacrifices one person to earn money and spends it to save the nation, it won’t be caught. This is also a law of public governance. Those who do so will not fail. 

I have become notorious for causing trouble in the world, but is it because of me? The ones who made it so are all of you here. Because you insisted on doing what the teacher said not to do, it became so. You all made it so that I would be blamed for what you did wrong, and now I am left alone to bear it all. (Laughter) 

The teacher has never been blamed for anything wrong. It is all because you did what you were told not to do. This mouth of yours is the enemy. Women gossip and talk about how our teacher is, and they say everything, even what they were told not to say. Many people who do not listen to such words are ruining the Unification Church. 

From the perspective of the spirit world, you are quite close to the teacher. You are in a position like that of a father and his sons and daughters. So sometimes, if you do not listen to the teacher’s words, spiritually, the teacher may hit you. You might say, “I got beaten by the teacher the other night. But that stick was a stick of love.” And you feel good about it. Even if you are hit by the teacher, you feel good about it, so others think it is strange. All sorts of rumors can arise. Although the teacher does not talk about it, there are many here who have spread rumors. 

Just looking at Yang Yoon-young, when she graduated from Ewha Womans University, the teacher said that it shouldn’t be done. Then she said, “What do you mean it shouldn’t be done? I received grace from it.” She went around making a fuss. But the grace she received was surely because the teacher said things that had not been said in Christianity until now. If he had said things that everyone already knew, would she have felt grace? With such things, she went around saying that all the good men and women of the Unification Church had gathered, and if you don’t follow, it will be a big deal, which made the established church members furious. Then that person, who used to be like that, now comes and says, “I’m having a hard time, so please support me.” Instead, they come to the teacher and throw a tantrum. But you can still throw a tantrum, so how happy are you? (Laughter) The most pitiful person is Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. The teacher has never learned how to throw a tantrum. He doesn’t even think about such things. When he sees such people, he thinks, “How great! They are doing revolutionary work.” 

The teacher does not exploit or gnaw at you. He absolutely does not do such things. This is certain. Therefore, it concludes that you need the teacher. You must be more patriotic than anyone in the Republic of Korea and must live to embrace humanity more than anyone in the world, regardless of life or death. 

When that historical foundation remains, anyone will follow that path with their life on the line. If a path can be paved from the individual to the world, history is a history that turns back, so all people will eventually find a way to live as one body. This is the teaching of the Unification Church. 

The desire of all things to hear laughter
You must manage all things publicly and establish public human relationships. Our factory used to work for seventeen or eighteen hours. Nowadays, it works for about twelve hours. While not paying much in wages, they ask for sacrifices and service. When the teacher talks about this, people say, “Oh, here we go again. The teacher is talking about sacrifice and service again. I heard it last year, and I’m hearing it again this year.” They complain. Those who have been there for more than three years are fed up! The teacher knows that immediately. So, if he thinks, “I shouldn’t let that person do that,” before long, they will withdraw on their own. 

Everyone is gathered to be assessed. They are given scores. When he speaks firmly based on the intention, they have no choice but to work hard again. The teacher can tell at a glance who is dozing off. 

When managing the factory to earn money, where do you spend it? Do you spend it for the teacher? The teacher does not own a house right now. He lives like this. When money comes in, the teacher first finds houses for those who follow him before thinking of getting a house for himself. He is setting conditions to be remembered before this nation and this people, not to be known or unknown. 

Do you know these principles? Raise your hand if you think this is wrong. As long as these principles remain and do not deviate, no matter how much you oppose or how much you wish for death, it will not die or fail. Rather, as time goes on, it will prosper. The teacher is laying a global foundation while receiving opposition. I no longer have anything to envy. If I were to say right now to send a Benz to the family in Germany, I would send it. 

Do you understand what I mean? Once a special order is given, there is nothing I cannot do. That is not the issue. However, to do that, a foundation that can benefit the nation must first be laid to create an environment where there are no side effects. 

Thus, a time must come when all things can be managed publicly. When that time comes, perhaps things will thrive without even giving fertilizer to the land. All things want to hear laughter every day; they do not want to hear crying. Raise your hand if you want to hear crying. The teacher does not want to, but I don’t know about you. It seems you don’t want to hear crying. You resemble me. Then raise your hand if you like to hear laughter. Everyone is raising their hands. Then how about God? God also likes to see laughter. Everyone is destined to live happily. 

If God is good, where is goodness? It is in living happily. It is as a subject with eternal authority that can digest everything with laughter.
The one who is present is God. God can digest even the worst things into something good, which means that what is bad can be considered good. If that happens, the principles of heaven and earth may change, but that is not the case. People say that the principles of the current world are not all meant to be lived positively. However, that is not true. The teacher argues that.

The world is made up of correspondence and opposition. If there were only correspondence, the world would be one. Everything would stick together. However, because of opposition, it can become a unique truth. In order to establish a discerning standard of existence, there must be conflict. That is how it works. This conflict does not end with just conflict; it is a conflict that can deal with corresponding existence. People do not understand this. In terms of philosophical thought, the theory of the Unification Church can greatly contribute to the new era.

Be the true owner of all things.
Considering all of this, you must respect public management. You must respect things if they are things. When the teacher was young and wrote in a notebook, he did not start writing from the lined part but from the very top. Sometimes he would write twice on one page. Then he could use one more notebook. You must use things sparingly.

The teacher is quite stingy about himself. Until now, he has never readily had a suit made. He only wore one after being urged to do so from the side. If he had gone in and had it made himself, he wouldn’t have enjoyed wearing it. When someone urges him to wear it and praises him, it is good to feel that he looks nice. Asking himself if it looks good after wearing it alone is self-promotion. The teacher does not do such trivial things. That is how the teacher’s nature is.

What kind of person does God like? God likes those who take public management as their philosophy of life. This is the same for all things. This is the principle of heaven and earth, the heavenly law.

People in the world may think that just because they attended university, they can arrogantly talk about others, but the teacher feels awkward and cannot play such games. If he dies, he dies, but he cannot do it out of awkwardness. Even though you come to greet the teacher of the Unification Church, if someone comes in a pompous manner, he wants to run away from that spot. Even now, there are times when he can intuitively feel the heart of the person greeting him. At such times, even if he receives the greeting, he feels unpleasant about it. You might think it’s unfortunate to feel bad about a greeting, but it is that the greeting itself feels unpleasant.

However, the teacher cannot resist those who are sincere. So far, while leading the Unification Church, when there are two people, and it comes to solving who among the two is better, he does not look at who has a good face but rather where their hearts are directed. In other words, he looks at whether it is private or public.

If you walk the public path centered on these principles, you will never fail. You will never fail, absolutely. Therefore, you must manage things publicly, treat people publicly, and serve heaven publicly. If those who do this well come together and form couples, then centered around that family, a new nation and a new world will be formed. Thus, you must become those who live a more public life.

Every time you welcome the Day of All Things, you should think about how much all things have longed for this one day throughout history. Therefore, you must be grateful for all things, cherish them, value them more, love them, and embrace them to become the true owners. To commemorate this day with the heart to become such a person means that you are qualified to understand the significance of the day God has come and to welcome this day. Do you understand?

<Prayer> Father, all the days until now have flowed with sorrow. Therefore, we bear the responsibility not to let the days that come flow with sorrow. We are the members of the Unification Church who have the mission to eliminate the misfortune that dwells in this country and to plant hope and aspiration.

In this current historical trend filled with despair, discouragement, grief, and sighs, we have come to understand that we must be the unifying Lord who can overcome this and leave behind new hope and aspiration. We earnestly wish and hope to be your sons and daughters who know that in order to walk that path, we must seek and live for more public values.

Father, there have been many sad stories in the process of the Unification Church coming out according to your providential will. There have been times when we were caught in circumstances that we could not tell anyone about, and we wanted to curse that there was no Father as we stomped our feet. Every time we think of those past days, we feel indescribably anxious and impatient, and we realize once again how pitiful you are as you have gone through time.

You have raised your face for us and have raised your hands and feet for us. Moreover, we know that you are our Father who has shed tears, blood, and sweat through countless arduous public connections for us. When we think about the fact that you are living with us within our realm of life, our hearts must be filled with the earnest desire not to let go of your hand forever. We must be filled with the desire to follow you along any path, whether it be a mountain path or any other path. When we have such a connection, even if we are lacking in strength, the heart that we must live carrying you will dominate us, and we will come to know that we have fulfilled the duty of filial piety and loyalty.

Father, as we recall the 1960s centered on the establishment of the Day of All Things, we remember the moment when we had to decide whether to go left or right at the turning point of a battle that no one knew about. That moment of blessing, that moment of forming connections, was a tense moment, a valley among valleys. That was a place where loving parents opposed, siblings opposed, and relatives with loving connections opposed. Standing in that valley where everything was lost, we welcomed you and began the history of the Unification Church centered on the value we found instead.

Following that connection, the Day of Parents, the Day of Children, and the Day of All Things were established. The day established based on these days is God's Day. This Day of God should become the Day of All Things, the Day of Children, and also the Day of Parents, but we realize that the glorious day that should have been achieved in one day has been patched together with intervals. Every time we welcome such a day, we cannot help but repent in our hearts for the mistakes made by the ancestors of humanity behind it. Father, please forgive us. 

Even though the silk of the full width should be immeasurably valuable, we must feel ashamed that it has become like a patched-up garment. Every time we welcome this day, we must kneel and shed tears, sympathizing with your pitiful self, and even if others cannot be filial, let us be the ones who vow with gritted teeth and bitten tongues that we will fulfill our filial duty. 

Every time we welcome this day, let us be your sons and daughters who realize that many people make such vows and that there is a true intention to commemorate this day. Father, we earnestly wish and hope for this.

Father, is there a son or daughter who has resolved that once they hold your collar, they will never let go? Not only the collar but also if they hold your wrist, even if their own hands fall off and their bodies become twisted, they cannot let go of your wrist, saying that they will hold it with all their life. Is there a son or daughter who, embracing your neck and resting in your arms, cannot leave forever, fearing that they might lose it, even if it means dying or failing? 

Even if they seem pitiful and have lost everything in worldly terms, is there a son or daughter who possesses the value of a standard that no one else has, capturing all the connections of heaven and earth and being able to move all the contents, knowing that the basis of all value dwells there, living only for that, boasting only of that, and exalting only that? 

Even if worldly matters flow away and social environments change, is there a son or daughter who knows for sure that the heart does not change and that it will inevitably create history and create environments? We earnestly wish and hope that there will be many of your sons and daughters who know this.

Father, please bless the path we Unification Church members are taking. Until now, we have all been bare. We became bare for you, so even if we are destined to die from being naked, we must be grateful. Let us be your sons and daughters who can be thankful that such a place has not appeared before us, imagining ourselves being stabbed by the spear of the enemy with our frozen bodies.

Today, let your sons and daughters gathered here not only understand the Day of All Things literally. Let them understand that it is not all things that are the problem, but rather the person who can follow all things, and that the problem is whether that person can follow you, Father. Let them understand that all things want to be governed and managed by a true person who can do so. 

Let your sons and daughters who love the world and all things become those who deeply understand the value of all things and can manage all things. We earnestly ask and hope for this.

Father, please bless your sons and daughters gathered on this day, and remember those sons and daughters who are widely engaged in missionary work around the world. May you repay the tears they have shed a thousandfold, ten thousandfold, and protect them, we earnestly hope for this. Even if we encounter the painful reality of hunger, even if we face a raging environment, let us go to you, and when we are in such a place, Father, we earnestly hope that you will be with us with your compassionate hand. 

Even if we are a foreign nation where emotions do not connect, let us be connected to you and establish a father-son relationship.

When we think that we must walk a lonely path of faith, even if the enemy's gun is aimed at us, let us understand that we have a responsibility to restore, and guide us in advance. We earnestly hope and wish that you will leave this country as a nation and people that you are with.

We know that there are many spirits in the spirit world who have gone there with regrets, having tried to find this day but unable to find the reality on this earth. Please grant them special envoys who can cooperate for goodness and bestow upon them the glorious grace to cooperate in establishing good customs on earth.

Let all humanity on this earth become your sons and daughters who know how to run the path of faith without sparing their lives to establish the will of goodness. Illuminate their paths, guide them, and show them the line of your life. Thus, let them become your sons and daughters who can welcome you with joy at the end.

Please hold onto the tired or fallen sons and daughters who are walking this path. Guide their steps, and even if they drink the bitter cup of defeat, do not let them become those who look to tomorrow with a heart of revenge, but let them be sons and daughters who look forward to the opportunity for recovery with hope.

The many people of the Republic of Korea, especially the Christian believers, have many sins. We earnestly hope and wish that you will forgive them for their disbelief and persecution against the Unification Church, as they did so out of ignorance.

We know that we cannot welcome this day joyfully with the enemy before us, so we hope that the world will welcome this day as a holy day to seek forgiveness and worship you, Father.

Until the remaining days and this world remain in your glory, your mercy, and your love, may all humanity not perish, and may the sons and daughters gathered here become victorious sons and daughters who can welcome that day. We earnestly ask for this, and we pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

Responsibilities of Blessed Families
Looking at the activities centered around your families, there are many things that need to be corrected. In your families, there will be children born before the blessing and children born after the blessing. However, the children born after the blessing should be the models in our church, yet there are many cases where they do not become models. Generally, there is such a tendency.

Blessed families must fulfill their responsibilities.
Ultimately, we cannot help but think that the parents have not fulfilled their responsibilities. In other words, the result of the parents not fulfilling their responsibilities toward their children in family life or church life has caused significant hindrances to their faith journey. Unless these issues are corrected, I want to say that we cannot overlook the blessing issues of established families in the future.

Considering such issues, once you become parents, you must take responsibility for teaching your children about the life of purpose. Blessed families must not only establish children of faith centered on purpose but also fulfill their responsibilities toward their own children.

June 4, 1970 (Thursday), at the former headquarters church.
* This message was given at the founding general assembly of the established families, and the title was added by the editor.

Blessed families bear dual responsibilities.
You have children of faith, children born before the blessing, and children born after the blessing. They truly embody the forms of rebirth, growth, and perfection, and how to educate these children is the most complicated issue. If you do not solve this issue exemplarily in the future, will it not have a significant impact on the many families that will receive established blessings and their children? I see this issue as an important responsibility that you must bear.
