The Hardship of God and Humanity  
We, who must pass through this fallen world, cannot help but be the most pitiful beings. When we stand in a position to escape the realm of the fall and try to break through reality toward the hope of the future, all environments that appear cannot be favorable, cannot cooperate, and cannot comfort those who wish to walk such a path, which goes without saying.  
Because this is the path we must walk in life, it is universally expressed as a lament. It is a sorrowful sea, a lonely sea, a pitiful sea, and a fearful sea. We cannot help but use the expression of lamentation because we feel the threats and urgency that can determine the judgments of life and death.  
Let us consider a person who wishes to walk this path of lamentation from a third-party perspective. In an environment like a lamentation, as he sets sail on a boat, a storm awaits him, and a raging current that swallows countless lives blocks his way. In such a situation, if there is a living being resembling a small boat, how lonely, pitiful, and miserable must be the path he takes? Yet, if there is someone who does not know such a path and departs, would not those who know it try to stop him a thousand times? But can that work be stopped? The fate of fallen humanity is such that they are in a position where they cannot be stopped.  
Behind those who know that path, there is a heart filled with concern, worry, and deep sorrow before they bless the path of those who wish to depart from it.  
From this perspective, how must God feel as He looks upon this fallen world, this universe trapped in pitch-black darkness, and humanity without direction or standard? God knows how humanity should walk but cannot teach them. Yet, we humans are in a position where we must walk. We must recognize that until now, there has been an indescribable misery, sorrow, and hardship between these two.  
How great must that hardship have been? There must have been hardships beyond the limits of your own hardships, which you cannot feel even after living your entire life. If there was pain, injustice, and fear, that too is something unimaginable for us humans. That fear, injustice, and sorrow do not exist without reason. There must be some basis for it. Then who is the subject that can be that basis? It cannot be anyone but God.  
God has stood in such a position until now as the parent of humanity.
Direction was presented. When God comes to us, presenting direction and giving commands, He must do so with the hope that we will achieve victory, knowing that we will surely go forth. However, have we become such a God? When we consider this, we realize that many righteous individuals who have come to know and follow His will on the path of restoration have gone through the ties of failure from the very beginning. Therefore, how much more pain must God have felt while watching this, and how much more loneliness must He have experienced? We cannot help but think about these issues.

When God commands one person to go, and that person cannot go, three others must be mobilized. If those three cannot go either, then countless others must be mobilized to ensure that the mission is accomplished. This is an inevitable destiny. If something intended fails once, it must be attempted again, and if it fails again, it must be tried once more. However, that command can only be given once. Heaven cannot issue another command simply because of failure. You must understand that this is the path of following God.

Thus, as we go through history, the closer we get to the time, the more we should teach the many prophets of the historical age, yet this has not been done. There is only one time when commands can be given from an absolute position towards the absolute. Because God is absolute, He cannot teach us again. However, if humans fail to carry out that command, God must ensure that it is fulfilled by any means necessary. Even if it is fulfilled, it remains God's achievement, not humanity's, which means God must once again build a bridge to relate to humanity. You must understand that God cannot avoid the path of the pioneer to build that bridge.

The issue of overcoming the waves of death and prayer
If one person fails to fulfill their mission, that mission does not end with that one person. It is an issue that is absolutely accountable before God, so until it is accomplished through one person at some point, God will silently continue to work through countless times and efforts. When we think about this, was there a truly patient person who could break through the difficult and fearful environments of the historical age? You must realize that there has not been such a true person.

The truth exists only in God. There cannot be two truths. Therefore, we cannot deny the fact that only God is true. Until now, many prophets have claimed to live for the truth and for the sake of the truth, but what they have been living for has not been the truth, nor has what they longed for been the truth. We reflect on the fact that they left behind history from such a position.

You are like a solitary ship embarking on a lonely voyage. Accordingly, depending on your circumstances, you will encounter waves and storms. Do you have the conviction to push through such environments? Is your purpose clear as you head toward a particular harbor? Do you have the belief that you can enter into that environment, in other words, do you possess the confidence and conviction to overcome all conditions of sorrow and death?

Thus, how great a threat will come upon me? And how much have you longed for the image of being able to overcome and rise above that threat, to be able to praise from a third-party perspective? This is an unavoidable issue. Therefore, we emphasize absolute faith. Once you believe, have an absolute faith that no one can interfere with, and once you make a resolution, practice it absolutely. This is what the faith world, which has been presented before humanity while walking with God toward one purpose, must understand.

Only through absolute faith and absolute practice can this be overcome, right? If you despair during the process of going, you will not meet the world of purpose, the time of hope. If you do not overcome the approaching environment, you will not meet the time of hope. Therefore, the cause that can lead to reaching the goal must be absolute faith and absolute conviction practiced. This alone can be the content that overcomes even the waves of death.

Practicing this should not be done leisurely while looking ahead. It must be an exemplary practice that stakes your life in the moment of life or death, where every second counts. Only then will there be a possibility of overcoming that difficult hurdle; otherwise, even the possibility will disappear. You must be fully aware that this concern leaves a historical record in your life.

In this position, you must know that God surely exists and that what is needed is prayer. The prayer here is not a habitual recitation of scriptures, but a prayer meant to make judgments and decisions. You must understand that prayer is presented as a key point that can determine whether the pulse of your life is extended or not. You need to think about these issues. How many times have you earnestly prayed before God in such moments? This is a significant issue that each of you must leave behind in your faith life.

The foundation of eternal life
If someone comes to this earth and faces the moment of destiny, and if they repent of their past, all the facts of the past will pass through their mind like images. They will know who they are without anyone telling them. With the life they inherited from their ancestors, the environment they have been connected to until now, and all the stories they have left behind, everything from the past will appear in their heart at the final moment of their life.

Among those, if there is someone who says, "There was truth. I left something more precious than my life," then even if they came to this earth and left, they will be someone who leaves behind a worthwhile moment. However, there are also those who simply pass through this life like a passerby. When recalling the stories of such people, if all those stories are filled with memories they do not want to remember, they will be miserable. The more they recall the past, if their face is filled with joy and all their problems can be submerged in ideals, then even the fear of death will be adorned as a comforting scene for them.

In this light, the moment of recalling the past is not a moment of fear; if they left something else behind, their past will not be dead, and their reality will not appear as dead. A person with such a past must have a connection that their nation can follow, and they must leave a legacy that all people of the world cannot help but follow.

So what kind of story might that be? When there is a miserable and unjust time when a nation cannot solve its pressing problems, if there was a time when they risked their life to take responsibility and resolve that issue, it will be an unforgettable moment in their past. In the course of their life, if they went to the point of death for their brothers, relatives, or others, and if there was a time when they fought for their salvation, then those facts will appear as images in their heart at the final moment of destiny. No matter how many happy moments they had centered around themselves, and how many times they were welcomed by crowds and praised gloriously, those moments will not have any effect at that time.

When considering whether they were good, whether they were true, and whether they could stand alone before God, truth and goodness do not start and end with oneself. They must begin with oneself and bear fruit in others, or be initiated by others to bring results to oneself in order to be considered good. This is similar to the principle that all existence in heaven and earth must go through the relationships of giving and receiving.

If their past life was one of giving, there would be no fear even in the face of death. If they gave everything for others, sacrificed for others, and lived a life close to truth while shedding tears for others, and if they poured their life into others, then that past will be a shining past.

Longing for such a past, when thinking of the nation, the conclusion will be that a hopeful nation must be like this. When they long for such a past, they can determine that the original goodness that sacrifices for others and hopes must be like this. Therefore, because I have a past of fighting for that, there must inevitably be a future that can be like that, and when I go before God with that content, it becomes the foundation of my eternal life. You must understand this.

The path of the sage is different from that of the ordinary person. The sage sought to live with history, with the world, and with the future. However, the ordinary person sought to live for themselves and to make the world exist for their own sake. For the ordinary person, thinking of the past brings darkness, but for the sage, thinking of the past brings light. What is that light? It is the ability to envision a hopeful nation. Therefore, if there is a hopeful heaven, that heaven must begin with them. That is heaven.

When you draw a diagram of how you are moving in this fallen realm with its harsh environment, you may predict that one year will go this way and another year will go that way, or that ten years will go this way and ten years will go that way, planning your life path according to your own standards. Those who rise and fall based on themselves will find that when they face their final destiny, everything they lived for themselves while sacrificing others will bind them.

Isn't the burden of conscience what binds the self? If one has lived a life burdened by conscience for more than half their life, that will bind them tightly for more than half of their existence. If such a life has been lived, they will stand in an indescribably miserable position at the final path of destiny, won't they? When we consider this issue, if the diagram of that life is drawn for the sake of goodness and for others, then no matter how low it may have fallen, it cannot become sorrowful. Humanity must pursue such a life path, which is why human ethics and morality also call for such a path. You must understand this fact.

How to overcome this contradictory environment
Is the path of going for others an easy one? It is not easy. It is not an easy path. If the path for oneself is not easy, how much more difficult is the path for others? You must understand that it is even more difficult. Therefore, if fallen humanity simply continues as it is, it is needless to say that they will not escape from the fallen world.

Living just for oneself will not allow one to escape the fallen realm. Because they were born in a fallen environment, living centered on oneself will only lead to disappearance. Therefore, to escape this realm, one must strive. To inevitably escape, a revolution must occur. There must be a struggle.

Many conditions will come into play. Those matters will not be things that can be welcomed with a nod. This path must be taken with hands trembling and bodies twisting. That is why this path is a path of suffering and sorrow.

The environment you find yourself in within the fallen realm is a contradictory environment. To break through that contradictory environment, you must overcome it. You must fulfill the mission of a vanguard that can receive the command to advance into that environment. You must understand that this is the path of our lives that must move with such a command.

Therefore, humanity must leave behind a life centered on oneself. The way of the sage is not a life for one's own personal life or for one's parents and family. It is a life that departs from that, a life that lives for one's nation, a life that departs from living for one's tribe, a life that departs from living for one's country, and further, a life that departs from living in this fallen world.

So where will they live after departing? There is no place to live after departing. There is no place to live except in this world. However, if there is one method, it is to create a good world and live as the owner of that good world. Therefore, you must understand that humanity calls upon God and longs for truth.

Thus, we must live for God. To do so, we cannot compromise or trade with this world. The connection must be established from a realm that has broken through the boundaries of the world.

So, looking back at the historical age thus far, has there ever been a time when the boundary was broken? There has not. That is why there are still sad conditions remaining. History is still in the night, not having passed midnight, and is looking for dawn, which is why sorrow and sadness linger. We must realize that this is the historical age we are in.

When we consider history thus far, humanity has not known the direction they should go. They are wandering within the realm of their environment, not knowing where they came from or where they are going. In such a situation, the struggles of individuals do not stop with themselves but extend to their environment and even to the world. You must understand that we are in a reality that leaves behind a destiny to conclude this history of struggle.

What should we do at this crossroads? This is the question. We have an inner desire to break through this crossroads and aspire for noble life. This desire is something that cannot be discarded, but because it is difficult to fulfill, life is called a bitter struggle. Therefore, historically significant individuals have sought new connections while traversing the path of life and death. This has been their lifestyle and way of thinking. That is why issues such as philosophy, religion, the absolute, and God have emerged. We know well that these issues have become factors from which culture has formed and traditional origins have been established.

When we think from that perspective, you have not become a person who can transcend the historical age. You must become one who holds onto the historical age and leaps over it. This cannot end here. You must break through and transcend this by relying on any strength. You must overcome and surpass this. This is the path of the way that sages walk. If religion must exist, then that religion has a significant responsibility to resolve these issues along with the final destiny.

You must experience the realm of self-transcendence.
So have you transcended the individual? Have you transcended the family? Have you transcended society? Have you transcended the nation? Have you transcended the world? These are questions that cannot be answered in a moment.
If there is a person who can feel, be stimulated, and experience, he is a serious person. Once one enters such a state, he inevitably becomes as lonely as it is serious. That position is not one that anyone can sympathize with. It is not a position where anyone can become a friend. It is not a position where anyone can travel together. In this way, the abyss of death that I alone must live, decide, and resolve is laid out before you. You must keep this in mind.

When you think about how to seek a moment of liberation from this abyss of death within your living space, the path to find this method is the path of virtue. If there is someone who steps onto this path of virtue, from the moment he steps onto that path, how serious will he be? It will not be a casual step back and forth. It will be a step that crosses the critical point of life and death. His essence will be an entity that acts with a resolute heart to cross that critical point with such a desperate mindset. 

The problem starts from here. The moment he crosses that critical point, it will undoubtedly be a moment when the pulse of life is moving intensely. There, one must know the misery of life and cast off all the burdens of life's stories and pains. That moment will be one where a new cry can be heard, and that position must be a place of intense internal struggle. Moreover, along with that struggle, the cry of "Oh God! Father!" must cross your lifeline and reach a new world where it collides. Have you ever called out to the Father with such a heart?

If you cannot stand in such a position, even if the door of true religion is opened in all directions, you cannot pass through that door. That door can only be opened through such a process, so to pass through that door, you must have a more desperate heart for life. 

That is why the Unification Church emphasizes sacrifice. It is also about seeking to enter a place that is infinitely deep if it is deep. You may experience a moment in a quiet night when it feels like the whole world has disappeared, and only the sound of your own pulse can be heard. You must reach a state where you feel that pulse moving and encouraging the life force of all your cells. Furthermore, you must reach a state where you forget even that pulse and, with a heart that is unaware of whether I exist or not, like a projectile shot towards a target, you can infinitely run toward it and bind the ties of life in your heart, reaching a state where if you fall, you fall infinitely, and if you are dragged, you are dragged endlessly, colliding with the fallen world and shattering it to pieces. You must reach such a state; without reaching that state, you cannot break through and transcend this realm of death to reach the new world of victory.

You must understand that such a state cannot exist within the realm of physical stimuli that are entangled in the complex and harsh social environment and emotional experiences of today. To enter such a state, you must earnestly seek a target with infinite life force in a place that is infinitely deep and infinitely quiet. 

As you go infinitely deep, when you feel that it is absent, you must encounter an existence of greater value than anything in heaven and earth. Thus, when you have the belief that even if I disappear, I can still say that I exist, the self that has lived until now will be resurrected there as a different self. Such a state cannot exist in today's complex and harsh social environment. That is why prayer is said to be done in secret. You are told to anoint your head with oil and pray in secret. Those among you who have had such experiences will know the value of prayer.

The three days of suffering of Jesus

There is a path that cannot be fallen into even if someone tries to lead you to fall; a path that is naturally admirable; that path is the source of my life, and that path is the subject of my life. Only those who want to possess this and connect with it, and who long for such a life, have the possibility to transcend the realm of death today, right?

Jesus said, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will." The moment of that prayer was not like any ordinary moment. Tears would have flowed from his eyes, and sweat would have poured from his whole body, arising from his marrow. Even if he gave strength, it would have been a strength beyond life and death.

Though it was a short few words before the Father, those words were the final voice that arose from his bones, weren't they? "Father, why have you forsaken me?" The place where he said that is not an ordinary place. Even though he had devoted himself to finding a connection with the Father, he earnestly prayed about what the Father's will was, which he could not forsake. The hidden light of a thin thread of hope behind that was the cry that arose from his heart.

When we look at this issue, we must surely seek such a state. It may seem like nothing can be grasped there, but it is absolutely impossible for there to be nothing. Once something is grasped there, it is something you do not want to let go of for a thousand or ten thousand years. So what will that which is grasped there become? It could be the Father's shoulder, it could be the Father's arm, or it could be any hem of clothing connected to the Father. When you grasp it and pull it, if you do not get pulled along, he will come to you, and it will be a time when you can roll over with God. Such a time must be present before individuals.

That is why those who have walked the path of virtue until now have entered the mountains and practiced asceticism. They did not do it to eat and play. They did it to devote themselves. Then how much devotion is required? What is the limit of that devotion? It is first entering a state of no self. This state of no self is not entered from an ordinary position. If you are standing in a position where you have fallen into the lowest valley and bear the burdens of the difficult world, then you have borne the greatest burden and are the most pitiful, and it is from such a position of utmost desperation that you can enter.

From such a position, you must seek out to start anew.

What does it mean that Jesus suffered for three days after he died? Because heaven and earth remain in the realm of death, and hell also has a connection to the realm of death, Jesus had to transcend this realm of death both below and above to govern heaven and earth. Therefore, even if he had to suffer in a place like hell at the very bottom, he had to pursue the ties of life and walk the path of hope that could comfort God.

Thus, by passing through that hellish environment, a path was prepared for Jesus to restart toward the kingdom of hope, and although he was forsaken and persecuted on earth, he was able to leave behind a path of hope.

That is why Jesus could not avoid the three days of suffering. We must understand this fact.

What did Jesus do alone for three days? He must have prayed with a deep intensity that pierced to his bones. Then, can two people go to such a place? No, that place cannot be entered by two. There is only one absolute counterpart to the absolute. You must understand how pitiful God is, who is calling us from that absolute position.

When you enter such a place and call out, "Father!" you can know the Father who has traversed a thousand years without having to learn about him. That place is indeed a place where you can experience the Father's toil and suffering without learning about it. Is that moment not the moment when you can grasp the Father's heart in your heart without anyone teaching you? Is that heart that calls out "Father" not the moment when an eternal bond can be formed? Therefore, many words are not needed there. The heart that has found the lost Father, that attitude, is the final prayer, isn't it?

What is the highest purpose of God's providence that has been unfolding for humanity until now? It is to find the Son as a Father. The place where the Father can say, "My son, so-and-so!" is the ultimate goal, and that is the point where all problems can be solved in the end. That place cannot be achieved without prayer.

In going toward that place, there must be a point where the absolute world and the realm of death intersect. This is because one cannot simply enter such a state. To become a son of God, one must go to that intersection and connect with a path that can proceed from there, and there, if there is God's heart and the sorrowful heart of God, it must be able to resolve it. Only from such a position can one feel the joy of resurrection and meet a moment of liberation to become an heir of the kingdom and be able to go to the kingdom.

Then the question is, how do we overcome the realm of death that is engulfed in fear? Within this realm of death, we must hold onto the thread of connection with God, even if we struggle, fall back, or enter a deeper valley of circumstances. There must be a master who can hold onto that thread, someone who supports me, and someone who can help me overcome difficulties.

Do you have even a thread connected to God while living on this earth? Are you living transcending the environment of this earth? When you think about these issues, you are all just a bunch of rascals, aren't you? Therefore, what you need is prayer and devotion. Have you stood in the place of resurrection? If you have not, have you at least stood in a place where you can earnestly ask? Have you become someone who can take responsibility for the environment while having faith? We have not. That is why prayer is important.

Prayer has the active ability to move the standards of life and death. To pray in such a way is a difficult task. If I were to build a wide tower, a tower a thousand feet high, how busy would I be? To build a wide and tall tower, how busy would I have to be? If I decided to build it over fifty years, would there be any time to rest? No.

Fear will come crashing in from around. There will be the fear of nature, the fear of the environment. In this fallen world, it is not just about building a tower of devotion. If you build it, Satan will repeatedly knock it down. If you build one, he will destroy two. Therefore, we must build while fighting against Satan. 

In such a fate, do we have any time to rest? We, who bear the mission of building this while serving God and facing Satan, cannot afford to rest even for a moment until the end of our lives. Is that not so? You must not let your guard down until you reach your destination across the sea of fear.

Pray without ceasing

If there is a way to die for God, it would be a happiness to die. If there is a way to die for God, it would not be a problem to cut off my life. When I look back at the trials I have felt inside and outside until now, if I can become someone valuable who can walk this path to the end, then the path of death is not a problem.

Now, in light of this issue, are you currently in such a position? The path to the kingdom of heaven is connected in such a way. Do you understand? You must go back through the 6,000 years of history along that path. Therefore, you must live with God. There is only one relative position that can connect with the absolute. For the world of Satan and the world of heaven to become one, they must first intersect. To cross over to the world of heaven from that position, you must let go of the ties of reality. That is why Jesus also said to pray without ceasing.

Members of the Unification Church often say that once you reach perfection, you no longer need prayer. This is a serious mistake. They speak well, saying that once you are perfected, you do not need prayer. That is indeed true. However, the standard of that perfection is to restore the nation. That position is where Jesus fulfills his wishes. Jesus intended to unite the nation of Israel with Judaism to emerge as the central nation of the world. That position is the place of perfection. You must understand this.

When an individual reaches perfection, he can stand as an individual, but the family’s Satan remains. When the family is perfected, the tribal Satan remains, and when the tribe is perfected, the national Satan remains. This is how it is, but does everyone become perfect as soon as they enter the Unification Church? To reach perfection, one must pray earnestly. You must pray as the teacher prays. The closer the time gets, the more the teacher is engaged in earnest prayer.

You may not realize how desperate the time is right now. Those who bear the responsibility at the forefront of the restoration providence feel that which arises from their bones in a way that no one else knows. If you have realized that it is such a time, then you should not waste time foolishly. You must engage in earnest prayer. Sleep is not the issue. For a tree to grow well, its roots must go deep. To deepen the roots, one must undergo suffering that no one knows about and walk the path of toil. This is essential.

Members of our Unification Church tend to boast a little when things go well. They also complain and make excuses. Such people cannot be the roots. They can only be leaves. Leaves can easily show up as soon as they sprout, but roots do not show themselves. The deeper they are, the less they show. To become a large tree, you must have deep roots. The roots of the Unification Church are deep. Even after believing in the Unification Church for decades, you still do not know the teacher. You know too little. The teacher is someone who has deep roots.

So what position are you in now? Would you correspond to the trunk? If there are those who have entered the Unification Church, met the teacher, and have a pure heart to walk this path, they should feel ashamed of those who came before them or those who are doing well. Some people are trying to go straight, while others are trying to go sideways. If we go like this, there is no way forward. Everything will fail.

Even if you have come this far, if you fall away, that is the end. When you go out and come back in, you must feel great pain. You must offer more than three times the loyalty than before. Thus, you must pass through the realm where God reproaches you and reach the position where He forgives everything. Then, after completely becoming one with God, you must reach a point where you cannot even recall your mistakes.

That is why those who return to the Unification Church often have many hardships. It is similar to falling backward; there are hardships. Even when others are doing well, the thought of what others might think of you can be burdensome.
The mind of the spirit keeps coming and going. How miserable is this?

**Atonement and Resurrection**

A person who enters the path of the way must walk the path of death until they die. After living, they must suffer to atone for the hardships they will face after death. It means that we should reduce the suffering that will last for countless years after death and atone for it while we are still alive on this earth. You all need to understand this. The path of the way is one that must eternally walk the road of suffering, and it is through walking this path of suffering on earth that we can atone.

You all know the term atonement, right? Atonement requires conditions. The conditions that the Unification Church speaks of today—without those conditions, can you be saved? You are people who have been saved through conditions, so do not boast. What is there to brag about? Blessings are also conditional blessings. You must cross the path of death. Since this is the world of death, you must cut off all ties to this realm of death. Everything in this world is close to Satan. Everything is contrary.

Until now, the Unification Church has only been rumored to be bad, but recently there was an article in the newspaper stating that the Unification Church is not bad, right? Some people say that Reverend Moon of the Unification Church has a lot of money and good diplomatic means. They also say that he is smart and has spent an enormous amount of money for the Unification Church. But I don’t even have money to buy lunch, so where would I spend it?

There has been a mountain of suffering to get to this point. Who carried the cross of that mountain? If Reverend Moon of the Unification Church did not carry this cross, God would have carried it. You must think that the moment is near when we must repent greatly while looking toward the future world. The moment when we must settle things greatly is approaching.

The moment to determine filial piety and loyalty and to declare it is coming, so I am extremely anxious. God asks Satan, "Do you know the authority of my beloved son and the path of his labor?" and we must have the conditions to say that He can bless my son with the glory of eternity. You must have such content. Then the world will pull you in.

Where are you currently situated? Centered around the Unification Church, where are you? Members of the Unification Church must match their steps with the teacher day and night, wherever they go. Until now, the teacher has not lived with just this head. He has lived pouring all his life into aligning with God and going in the direction God goes.

Now, the three (God, the teacher, and you) must be united. You must match your steps. Because the decisive content of life and death is at stake, the three must unite at that point. In other words, there is the resurrection of life at that point. That point is where the Father and the teacher become one, and where the teacher and you become one and can connect. That is where one heart and unity occur.

Therefore, you must live a life aligned with the will. To do that, you must know what the will is. You do not know this, so you are told to pray. If you pray, the teacher will surely appear and teach you. Do you understand? If you want to live a life aligned with the will, it must be different from the past. In the past, because it was a historical lineage, humans had to receive God's commands and take responsibility. Even if they received the command and took responsibility, God did not come down to this earth. Do you understand what I mean? In the past, it was a historical lineage, so even if humans received God's commands and accomplished that work, God could not come down for that work. Humans had to go up to God and offer it. Only after offering could the one responsible for that work come.

Do you understand what I mean? That is why I have been saying not to be arrogant until now.

**To Receive God's Praise**

Those who only think of their own affairs for their own sake will perish. Why will they perish? Because God is not interested in such matters. Even if you say you have accomplished something, you must go up to God and become one with that work and be a sacrifice. Only then can you be sent into the new era. This has been the content of God's providence during the historical lineage. Therefore, anyone who brings God must offer something.

Before receiving the blessing, you must first offer it before God. Then, return to yourself and ask how much you can offer. You must offer your nation and the world. Those who are responsible for running on the path of offering will become people who cause problems in the world.

If God commanded me to give 100, does He really want just that 100? I must give 120 percent of what God desires. If I offer even a little more than what is desired, He will say, "Good!" and praise me. This is where value changes. When God gives a command, can you offer your one and only life? Since you are in the position of being like a servant's child before God, can you be praised? When you receive a command of 100 from God, you must give more than that. This is the best method. If you do that, it will be glory for the individual and content that God can boast about. If you did what you were told and gave a million, that is something others can also do. Wouldn't that be the case?

You know there are records, right? There are records for the Olympics and other achievements. Those records can be broken, right? Therefore, if we only do a hundred, Satan can say, "God, that is something anyone can do." A hundred is something anyone can do. He can accuse us. Anyone can achieve that if they try. Therefore, we must strive for more than 100.

Looking at the historical era, God has brought forth many people. Some have given 100 percent, some 90 percent, some 80 percent, some 20 percent, some 10 percent, some 0 percent, some minus 10 percent, some minus 20 percent, and some minus 100 percent. Isn't that how it is? The content of responsibility varies greatly. This (100 percent) is a high position in heaven, and this (minus 100 percent) is a high position in hell. That is how it is.

When the teacher asked the Unification Church members to do something, it seems there are no such incompetent people. Since you cannot do that work 100 percent, among you, the teacher is the most incompetent. Since I gave the command, ultimately, I become the most incompetent person. That is how it works.

When the teacher says to do something, who is it for? It is for you. Do you understand that? If you do not do it, do I suffer? No. Because what the teacher asks you to do is something you can do.

Everyone here has come with a relative environment. You have come to sell the rag bundles left by your ancestors. You did not come to receive a value assessment. If your ancestors were good ancestors, you must act like good ancestors. If you do not, I will take away all of your ancestors' positions up to now. I will monopolize it. Therefore, I will not suffer any loss. I will take it all.

The season of harvest is coming soon, and you must bear fruit. If you do as the teacher says, you can bear fruit. If you think you cannot bear fruit, you must put in effort. You must do such work.

The teacher can forgive those who have committed grave sins. By what privilege? Because he has the privilege of countless ancestors. Until now, many practitioners have taken many bundles from me. Seeing that, the teacher is like a thief, right? He is the biggest thief. This is unavoidable. If it had not been this way, I would have already perished. The contract has been made that way.

In the historical lineage, one can come and go anytime and anywhere. One can go anywhere in the world. Isn't that right? However, this era cannot just pass as it is. Therefore, we have entered a time when we can atone for the historical lineage horizontally. At this time, there is no retreat. That is why there is no retreat on the path of Reverend Moon of the Unification Church.

**Become God's True Children**

Some people may say that the number of Unification Church members has decreased compared to the 1960s, but it is okay if it has decreased. The leaves of a tree become fewer in autumn than in summer. Is that right? Do they increase or decrease? When the wind blows, the leaves fall, and the branches become bare. That is normal. If only I remain, I will step forward. On that day, you must know that I will reap many times more than what you have worked for. That is the kind of self I have. Do you understand?

If you pray seriously like in the past, God will work. The teacher has that confidence. Therefore, whether it is in America, Europe, or anywhere abroad, such actions occur. No matter how large the audience is, I can grasp it in my hands. I possess such a method. Even if I go to an island inhabited by cannibals in Africa, I can live without being eaten. The teacher has something like that. Even in prison or in the wilderness, I have been someone who has evangelized with the cooperation of the spirit world.

God and you are originally in a rich relationship. In the New Testament era, humans were God's adopted children. But now, we are in a relationship of father and son, so what the son does is what the father does, and what the father does is what the son does. It becomes a joint action. What belongs to the father belongs to the son, and what belongs to the son belongs to the father. The Unification Church is frightening because it teaches this relationship of father and son. This is the most frightening thing.

You just want to open your mouth and receive for free, right? You must think about whether God is a real father. Who is the one who calls Him father? It is the sons and daughters, right? You must become God's true sons and daughters. Shouldn't you? Who do the sons and daughters resemble? They resemble their father and mother. They resemble their parents. And who do they live with? They live with their parents.

Even if you are thousands of miles away from your parents, you must resemble them. Do you resemble them? The way children run or walk is similar to their parents, right? That is true. They may not be exactly the same, but they are similar. The way they blink their eyes, the way they laugh, their body, the way they eat, and the way they sleep are all similar. Parents like to see their children resembling them. Isn’t that right? No matter how ugly a creature may be in the world, if a daughter or son resembles them, they will love that child more. That is how it is.

Today, the Unification Church teaches that a servant can resemble the master. When the teacher says, "Let’s do it!" it is not supposed to be a "No, I won’t do it." If you say you won’t do it, that is Satan. When God says, "Let’s do it!" which is better, to say "Yes" or to say "Ugh!"? If you are just blinking your eyes, would that be good? That is why there are servants, adopted children, and sons and daughters. What is there? There are servants, then adopted children, and then sons and daughters. This is the standard of restoration.

In the position where God is responsible, there is the authority of a servant, the authority of an adopted child, and the authority of a son. Likewise, there are also ranks of servants here. If a servant says to an adopted child, "You are incompetent," it is like a dog with dung scolding a dog with ashes. If an adopted child says to a son, "What kind of heir is that? That family is finished," it is the same case.

Then, if there is someone who immediately says they will go before the parents even before they say "Let’s go!" would that person be a son, an adopted child, or a servant? If someone is already stepping forward before the parents say "Go!" then that person is a son. The next person who hesitates and goes later can be seen as an adopted child. The person who says, "Hey, why are they going first and causing all this fuss?" is a servant.

Now, raise your hand if you want to be a servant. Who wants to be an adopted child? Everyone wants to be a son or daughter, right? To become that, you must resemble your father. You must resemble them in behavior, appearance, and in managing the household. Only then can you inherit. That is why today, the teacher of the Unification Church tells you to resemble God. Otherwise, you can only be an adopted child.

**Become Someone God Will Never Forget**

I have gone through many life-and-death situations, but I have never complained to God. 

"Why do you make me suffer like this? You said you would bless me?" I have not said that. How many promises do you think God has made with the teacher? Do you know how many? Hundreds of thousands of promises. "You will become like this." And at that time, I could not believe it. Every time, God brought evidence and promised, saying, "What is this?"

How much has God been deceived by humans? Isn’t that so? The fallen lineage that has a connection with the servant who deceived God is Mister Moon, so what can be done? How much has God worried about the teacher? That is why, fearing that I might not believe, He made all sorts of people bear witness before the teacher. Even while believing in such a God, I have endured torture and entered all sorts of sorrowful situations, yet I have not blamed God.

The teacher is a person who walks the path that humans must walk, that is, a person whom God desires, a person who can shed new tears that God has not seen until now. The philosophy of life of the teacher is to shed new tears that have not been shed until now and to die. How much heart did Jesus have when he died? The teacher must have a heart greater than that so that God can say, "You are better than anyone else."

If there is someone who has died for the father, not for others, the father will never forget that person, even if a thousand or ten thousand years pass. Shouldn’t we die with such feelings and content in such a position? If one dies while being beaten and bleeding for God, God will shed even sadder tears and feel more regret than this.

Then, at that time, God will leave a more sorrowful story through me than through anyone in the historical era, right? The teacher has made this my lifelong wish. In that sense, even if there are many people walking such a path among all the people of the world, can anyone be as much as the teacher of the Unification Church? There is none. I may not know about other things, but this is certainly true.

I know the path of restoration, and I pray to God, "Is this the path you must walk? Shouldn’t it be like this?" I do not pray about what has passed lightly. I will keep this path where the Father can be with me. The issue is how to establish a connection in this era for what must be accomplished in ten years, or even a hundred years, or a thousand years later. Also, how to sweat and shed blood for that time, and how to...
The issue is whether to set the conditions for effort. This is what the teacher has been exploring until now. Despite being the teacher who has come this far, those who oppose the teacher's call to go together will fail. Just wait and see if they fail or not.  
Those who act according to their own desires will be condemned by heaven. God is not governed by the sincerity of the greedy. Justice is not about submitting to the blade of a tyrant. Where is such a path? What kind of path is it? It is a path that must follow God.  
Until now, God has devised countless strategies to lead humanity along this path. While the heart may wish to go in a day, it has taken 6,000 years. Therefore, we must pave the way that can be traveled even in a day. To compensate for the standard of the fall that has compressed 6,000 years of vertical history into a single day or an hour, we must consider how much sincerity must be invested. Many people are following the Unification Church to walk this path. However, there are also many who bear burdens before the teacher. Many people criticize in various ways.  
There are many secrets in governing a nation. There are secrets that cannot be spoken even in a small family. How could there be no secrets in the process of restoring heaven and earth? There are secrets that cannot be revealed even in front of you. If these were revealed, no one would dare to walk this path. There are such secrets. You must understand that there are divine secrets that cannot be disclosed all at once.  
However, as you follow the teacher, you have been talking this way and that, causing the teacher to be criticized until now. There is no way that I am being criticized because of my mistakes. It is because you have made mistakes that I am being criticized. It is simply because of your mouths. What does it matter? That is your mouth. The path you must take contains a thousand years of stories, yet you are going around talking about this and that.  
Thus, the teacher has faced persecution until now. He has been carrying a ragged burden. He has taken on the crosses of those who follow him. God, who must gather and lead such people and bless them, feels wronged. You must understand this. God does not want to impose the cross on His beloved children; therefore, when difficulties arise, He only imposes them on those responsible, providing them with an environment that is not difficult. Yet, these thieving groups are causing a commotion. They all must perish. There are many groups that must perish. God does not reveal everything to all humanity. Only those who can take responsibility and move forward know it.  
Even now, do you know what is happening behind the scenes centered around the Republic of Korea at this very moment? You do not know, do you? To speak frankly, preparations for war are underway. Women may not know this. The entire world is like this. Then democracy will never be established forever. As long as there is an enemy, democracy will fail. It is always destined to lose in strategy.  
For example, Cambodia or North Vietnam may have advanced strongly but then retreated, so they will do anything. Democracy is currently engaging in extremely misguided strategies. Isn’t that right? When going to war, do they announce that they will fire artillery? Is there democracy even in war? Yes, there is, or is there not? Is there democracy in front of an enemy? Is there democracy in front of the blade of an enemy or a dictator? That is why God has never taught all secrets until now. You must understand this.  
So, are you who follow the teacher a hindrance or a collaborator? Those who speak excessively are hindrances. Those who have not directly experienced suffering and speak this way and that will be judged. You must understand that there will come a time when you must offer your life to compensate. There is a saying that goes, “Heavenly secrets leak.” If information leaks during a covert operation, it becomes a major problem.  
The more you serve a high person, the more issues you must be careful about as you get closer to them. That is why it is always said to bow your head and be cautious. You must be careful. Everyone who deals with the will must do so.  
When you approach the teacher, you must do so with a heart of earnest prayer. The teacher is discerning the connections of the heavenly world through this standard. You must always be careful with your words in front of the teacher. That is always the issue. Therefore, do not speak foolishly. You must conclude the realm of death from this position and align it with the realm of life. Thus, you must be life from birth until death. You must live like that. You must be born from heaven, live in heaven, and embrace heaven when facing death. To do this, you must go through prayer.  
The faith standard that Unification Church members must establish  
We Unification Church members like the word completion. The teacher himself has not yet reached the position of completion. To stand in the position of completion, the nation must be completely restored. However, our nation is currently divided into North and South. Therefore, I am praying while negotiating with God on how to unify this nation. Yet, you are playing by the water without even entering it, thinking that the will is being fulfilled without knowing the essence. This must not be the case. You must pray earnestly.  
So what is the difference between a Unification Church member and a traditional Christian? Until now, we have been praying desperately, shedding blood, sweat, and tears centered on the vertical history. Now is the time for the father to seek the son. Do you understand? Therefore, if you make a little effort, if you enter that realm for just a week and put in sincerity, everything will connect. Thus, you must serve the teacher as a child serves a parent and receive direct guidance from the teacher. If you pray, you will receive direct guidance.  
If your mother receives such revelations through prayer in your family, you must focus your sincerity on that mother. All family members should ask the mother what she received in prayer. That news will be the happiest news for them. Furthermore, it becomes an offering. From that, you can know whether that household will prosper or perish. When a mother prays in the family, God teaches about that family. Similarly, when you approach the teacher, the teacher will teach you. If you do so joyfully, something will happen. Just wait and see. If it doesn’t happen in a day, it will happen in three days; if not in three days, then in seven days; if not in seven days, then in three months; if not in three months, then in three years. If it doesn’t happen in three years, it will move to seven years. It is fundamentally structured to progress like that.  
Then, they will be able to sense what they were in prayer and prevent discord before it arises. Whether it is a joyful event or a sad event, something will happen. It differs from person to person.  
At such times, good things happen. At such times, difficult things happen. Everyone knows this. If you pray, you will surely be taught. It is set up that way. At that time, you must discern whether you are going down a good path or a bad path and choose the path you must take.  
That is why Unification Church members must receive direct guidance from the teacher through prayer or dreams. Among our members, there are many who receive direct instructions from the teacher wherever they go.  
More vivid events are occurring now than during the time of Jesus. We Unification Church members live directly with the teacher. In the Unification Church, there are often more significant events than during the time of Jesus. Because of such events, the world can unite with the Unification Church.  
Today, to pass through this realm of death, we must engage in desperate prayer. Prayer is not something done for just a moment. You can pray 24 hours a day. In this free era, those who cannot experience that and live without directly serving are pitiful.  
Blessed people originally have such standards and experiences, and everything must be connected to that content. Originally, one must be spiritually grafted to the teacher and become one to be a candidate for blessing. The principle of restoration is not to escape from the past in relation to the present. The facts of the past unfold as they are in the present. Therefore, the teachings of the Unification Church that teach about this cannot be anything but truth.  
Especially for women, without exception, they will be directly taught by the teacher in prayer. They must live serving the teacher. Then they will be taught through dreams. Those who have not seen the teacher in dreams do not qualify for blessing. The teacher must be seen in dreams. The number of Japanese members who approach the teacher in dreams is 70 times more than yours. From this, it can be seen that Japanese members are more earnest than you. If you are earnest, you will pray, and then you will be taught.  
The emotional standards that Unification Church members must have  
So how earnest must one be? One must be more earnest than a wife loving her husband or a lover longing for their beloved. This is the issue. If you live with such earnestness, even when you go to the spiritual world, you will remain within the limits of that heart, which is better than living in the world of Satan.  
Even a woman who used to live happily before entering the Unification Church, when she walks the right course and experiences the spiritual world, will naturally distance herself from her husband who was once close. That is why she faces ridicule. It is because her spiritual body is vigorously moving beyond Satan. However, this world is the world of Satan, and one cannot establish a relationship with God without overcoming the world of death. That is why the teacher is praying for you.  
Look, at first, the teacher is like a treasure, right? And he feels like a father. This is like Adam and Eve growing up in the embrace of their father. Next, he feels like an older brother, and then he is felt as a relative. If a woman cannot feel these three values, she cannot restore herself.  
That is why even if the women of the Unification Church try to cut off such feelings, they cannot. They absolutely cannot cut it off. What is cut off is false. That is why they can have strong experiences.  
There is a time when one feels like a father, and then there is a time when one can discuss and ask for help like an older brother. What is Adam? He is the spiritual father in the position of representing God. He is internally like a father to Eve and externally like an older brother. Then, when they unite and establish a relative relationship, they become a couple. Adam and Eve were meant to unite like that.  
Because the wives attending the Unification Church follow the teacher, their husbands complain that they do not come to their side, and conversely, women also complain that their husbands do not come to their side because they follow the teacher. This is how it is meant to be.  
Moreover, men must shed tears if they want to see the teacher. Those who cannot do so will not enter the kingdom in the era of the Unification Church.  
Because Adam, who could not feel God’s heart, was divided by tears, he must be united by tears, and the resentment of Cain and Abel, who were divided by tears, must be resolved by tears.  
Without that path, there is no way to unite. Even among men globally, there are those who cry wanting to see the teacher. But are there such people here? These fakes… In the past, everyone came out like that. Even in the early days, everyone did that.  
The Unification Church cannot take responsibility for restoration without establishing such conditions. In the past, no matter how much a man wanted to see the teacher, he could not endure it. There is a term called lovesickness, right? They were afflicted with that sickness. They were annoyed by anything in the world. They had to receive commands from the teacher to feel energized; otherwise, they could not find strength. That is how it must be. Are you all like that? Fakes… It must be done first.  
Then, how much must the Unification Church leader, who has such motivation and conducts such operations, long for God? He longed for God to the point of being unable to open his eyes, shedding tears to the extent that he could not see the sunlight. There was a time when he longed for God like that. You must understand this.  
To such a person, they call him a heretic or something. Let’s see who fails and who wins. If you know the content about the teacher, you will have nothing to say. Even if you go to the spiritual world, you will have nothing to say. Therefore, you must repay the debt you owe to the teacher. You must repay the debt you owe to your parents. The same goes for the teacher's position before God.  
If you quietly observe the women who are evangelizing, you will realize that behind them are good ancestors. You may have felt that often. They pray and take walks with their ancestors. They do so spiritually. Such processes must be undergone centered on emotional issues.  
The era of family restoration  
In this era, we must establish a completed Adam and Eve to restore humanity. Therefore, we must establish the laws of love through the connection of bride and groom, and there are countless heavenly laws and norms that must be followed accordingly.  
Do you think you can go to heaven with that?  
Now, this must be established in a familial way. It is time for parents to be served in the family, and for the father to teach the son. What purpose is the Unification Church centered around? It is a family church.  
God has fought until now to establish a woman in this world of Satan. Although God created a woman centered on a man, due to the archangel, the world fell. Therefore, in the process of restoring this fallen world, a woman must be established. The archangel was meant to serve Adam. However, it became a tragic world due to this archangel. The bridegroom Jesus also came to this earth for the sake of women. That is why beauty contests like Miss Korea and Miss World are being held. This is all because of such content.  
In the end, women will rise to prominence. That is inevitable. It fits perfectly. However, the people of the world do not know such internal core content. But at this time, when internal heaven and external earth, that is, the stories unfold, we must center families to create the entire world into one ideological world, right?  
The Republic of Korea is the central country that determines the fate of the world in the providence of restoration. In North Korea, they call Kim Il-sung their father, right? And in the Unification Church, we also call the teacher our father, right? This is the position of Cain and Abel. Then what will the Unification Church do? We must teach about God. That is why the teacher is trying to train many people.  
Will you receive training from the teacher? Will the men receive it?
Yes? "I will receive it." Those who are willing to receive it, please raise your hands. Put them down. I will teach you day and night. There is a law of heaven and a world of heaven. This is something you cannot understand unless I give you wisdom. You must prove the laws of the world through history and through the ages. So, how busy do you think that will be? The Communist Party will also get caught up in this.

Thus, the Unification Church in Korea must enter an era where it can determine the fate of the nation. It does not require a large number of people. About 300 people will suffice. While you are going up and down, the teacher has been continuously developing regardless of the environment until now. That is why I am teaching you this method.

Now, since it is a horizontal era, you must uphold the laws centered on God's heart. Do you understand? If you are a mother in the family, you must unite centered on the mother. The person who listens best to God's words in the family is Abel. If there is a difficult problem, you should pray. Pray boldly. How wonderful is that?

Now that we must establish a family-based life right, we must have one subject in the family and absolutely follow it. If the mother is on God's side, the father must also have a heavenly lifestyle and follow the mother. Thus, the father should wake up at dawn, curious, and ask the mother what the new message from God is. That is how it should be.

Pray continuously to become one.
The teacher does not need to ask others now, but those who are connected to heaven must provide testimony of three or more. That is the law of heaven. You must receive testimony from three or more and carry out your work. That is the problem.

That is why I call people who are connected to heaven and ask them. What is there to ask? I know everything. However, it is necessary. Because this time is urgent and we must go through relative environments, the teacher cannot do it alone.

Therefore, the teacher sets up three grandmothers to pray to lay the foundation of the church. Pray and become one. If you cannot become one, it will be a big problem. These grandmothers have sharp personalities and cannot become one. They are the most miserly among the miserly, and I have gathered people who cannot last three days in the world. They must become one. Only by becoming one can we solve all these various problems in connection with God, centered on heart. Since the Unification Church has a relationship of wealth, you must unite.

Then, whom should you resemble? Should the teacher resemble you, or should you resemble the teacher? You will not lose anything by resembling the teacher. The teacher does not live for himself. I have lived personally until now. Therefore, what is the most urgent issue for us now? It is to establish educational institutions. Do you understand? This is the most urgent issue.

How do we secure human resources to lay the foundation for the character of future generations? How will we create the best schools in the world from kindergarten to university? Therefore, the teacher will secure 1.6 million pyeong, which is about 400,000 pyeong larger than the 1.2 million pyeong site of Seoul National University. You may not think about it, but the teacher is preparing for that now.

You have sons and daughters, right? You are suffering now, but that is for your sons and daughters who will replace you in the future. Even if you suffer and sacrifice today, it will become a source of pride for your sons and daughters. That is why you are being made to suffer to the point of death for your sons and daughters. This is love. Therefore, no matter how much I push you, I do not feel guilty in my conscience. This is the right path. If you dislike it, try to pull back your tail. Then your sons and daughters will become a problem.

Go forward centered on the purpose. The initiative centered on the individual does not remain with the individual but must enter the family realm. The issue is how to form a family that can unify the world. That is why God has been laying the family foundation for 6,000 years. Therefore, you must adjust the environment and harmonize to achieve unity in your church life. To do this, you must understand that constant effort and constant prayer are necessary. Do you understand?

"Yes."
<Prayer> Father, as I reflect on the long history,
I think of your grace that has established my existence
and left me even in the midst of suffering. There are still many problems remaining, so I earnestly ask you to allow me to fulfill my duty of loyalty and filial piety.
How will a loyal subject meet the final day of victory? When will we be able to welcome you? We have come out determined to achieve that since the first night, and we are still running toward it. In our youth, we have offered this nation and this people before you, and we have lost all the fortunes of the nation that we could boast of to future generations. Now, over 50, the era of revival with this nation and people has come upon us. In the place of peace where all enemies have retreated, we will newly adjust our collars and dance before you, praising you and joyfully welcoming you.

Yet, despite this, enemies are blocking us, and today we face the final battle. I understand that the connections of 5,000 years of history have been led by you for a single purpose. I know that it is to establish a pivotal point for one nation, and that we cannot resolve this without disregarding the horrific path of blood that will be faced in the future of this nation. Only your love can resolve this, so a new movement must unfold on this land. Thus, the history of national revival must unfold on this land.

To achieve this, families that can represent the national revival must emerge. This is because there is a mission to ignite a fire from the family, concentrating the boundaries of this nation and state in the family and crossing over those boundaries. Moreover, from 1970 to 1972 is the most important period, so we have declared the period from May to October as a special prayer period. 

The time has come for us to truly love this nation, and we have reached the final critical path where we can serve the nation. Now is the time for us to hold onto this people and this nation and negotiate before you, Father. Please remove all conditions that prevent us from becoming one with you. When I think about how all conditions that Satan can accuse us of are tied up, I realize that this is a factor that can determine the final fate of this nation. How many sons and daughters are there who can fight for that, and how many families can do so? The more families and sons and daughters there are, the more I feel that the lonely son standing here must take responsibility for this.

Father, I have understood your heart, which has cried out in the painful crossroads of history. When I feel your circumstances and appear in that way, I believe that the connections of that emotion will establish an environment where we can rejoice beyond the sorrowful environment. I know that there have been many heartbreaking stories along the path you have walked until today.

Even if we step forward to take responsibility for this nation and this people in the future, I realize that you cannot freely entrust us with that responsibility. I have come to know that you are indeed a pitiful Father. There is no one on this earth who can sympathize with such a Father. The Unification Church is before a Father who is looking for a son who can comfort and embrace him, but is there such a son among this church? If there is such a son, I hope you will bless him a thousandfold and ten thousandfold. However, since there is no such person, I feel that I must take on the responsibility of carrying this cross myself.

Father, I have been struggling to create an environment where I do not cause you concern and where you can be pleased as I walk my path. However, when I think about how the nation cannot become one and the church cannot become one, leaving you with concerns and tears, I earnestly hope you will allow me to have an increasingly impatient heart as the time approaches. This is not because I do not believe in you, nor is it because I do not know your will. It is because I fear that I might leave behind conditions of concern after I go, so I earnestly ask you to allow me.

Father, I earnestly ask you to connect us to the life relationships we must establish as your sons and daughters. Among your sons and daughters gathered here today, are there any who have such families? Are they blessed families?

I know that our blessed families must be those who are crazy for your will, whether in dreams, in reality, or even in death. Our families must either become sacrifices or priests on behalf of the nation, yet there are many families that are not like that. When I think about that, I feel that I must take on the responsibility again for the blessings I have given. I also ask that you allow yourself to be in a position where you must take on that responsibility as well. Please gather and nurture them. For the blessed world of the future, I have no face to show, but I have no choice but to hide those wounds and faults and present them before you, Father. I earnestly ask you to allow that.

Please protect this nation and this people in the future. In this urgent situation, whether this nation will align itself with the world of evil or the world of good is at a crossroads. Please do not lose your guidance over the groups of unification that must determine the direction toward the world of good, and I earnestly ask you to bestow your grace of protection with your loving hand.

Please allow your deep internal love to be firmly established among the children who long for this day and offer their devotion for this place. Also, please allow us to establish a victorious lifestyle where you can be with us, so that we may be respected before many and take on a leading role in taking responsibility for life.

Father, please accept this day, and I ask you to accept this month and this year as your month and your year, and I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
